<!-- ==== FILE: web-tools/REGENERATE-PROMPT.md ==== -->
# Regenerate MineMGL Dependency Visualizations

> Copy-paste this prompt when phases change, scripts move, or new phases are added.

---

## The Prompt

```
Regenerate ALL THREE visualization files in web-tools/:

FILES TO UPDATE:
1. minemgl-grid.html — hierarchical grid (X=Phase columns, Y=Layer rows, nodes as rects, bezier edges, D3.js)
2. minemgl-heatmap.html — flat Phase×Layer coupling matrix (HTML table, cell drill-down, summary cards, coupling verdict)
3. minemgl-heatmap-3d.html — 3D extruded bar heatmap (Three.js, orbit controls, hover glow, click inspect, shadows+fog+rim lighting, ACES tone mapping)

WHAT TO DO:
1. Read every *.cs file inside learn/ (all phase folders: phase-All, phase-a-1(New), phase-b(New), phase-c(New), phase-d(New), and any NEW phase-X folders, plus handTyped(latest)/Scripts/phase-a for phase-a scripts).
2. For each script, extract:
   - Phase (which folder it lives in)
   - Layer (0-Core, 1-Managers, 2-Data, 3-MonoBehaviours, 4-Utils, 5-Tests)
   - All dependency edges by scanning for: class inheritance (:), interface implementation, Singleton<T>.Ins reads, GameEvents.OnX += subscriptions, GameEvents.RaiseX() calls, Get...() method calls on other scripts, Set...() method calls, new DataService() creates, UtilsPhaseX.Method() calls
3. Classify each edge as one of: inherit | interface | get | set | event-sub | event-raise | singleton | creates | uses-util
4. Rebuild the hardcoded JS node/edge arrays in ALL THREE files with fresh data from the scan.

RULES:
- Keep the existing dark theme (--bg:#101014 blue-black, JetBrains Mono, all bright edge colors — see color palette below)
- Keep all existing interactivity per file:
  - grid: search, edge type toggles, click-to-inspect panel, zoom/pan
  - heatmap: cross-phase-only toggle, cell click drill-down, summary cards, coupling verdict
  - heatmap-3d: Three.js OrbitControls, hover glow+scale, click inspect panel, tooltip, reset camera, cross-phase-only toggle, stats bar, legend, shadows, fog, ACES filmic tone mapping
- If a GameEvents partial was moved from phase-a to phase-All, update the node's phase accordingly
- Add any new phases as new columns (grid), new rows/columns (heatmap), and new axis labels + bars (3D) — assign color from palette
- The node data and edge data are hardcoded JS arrays in each file — replace them entirely with fresh data from the scan
- Every edge must correspond to a real code reference you verified by reading the file
- THREE.js is loaded via importmap from CDN (three@0.164.1), D3.js from CDN (d3.v7)

WHAT CHANGED SINCE LAST GENERATION:
[DESCRIBE YOUR CHANGES HERE — e.g.:]
- Added phase-e(New) with 15 scripts (machines: CastingFurnace, Sieve, ClusterBreaker, etc.)
- Moved OnMenuStateChanged from GameEvents(A) to GameEvents(All)
- Renamed ToolBuilder → ToolBuildingPlacer
- etc.
```

---

## When to use this prompt

- **New phase added** (phase-e, phase-f, etc.)
- **Scripts moved between phases** (e.g. GameEvents events promoted to phase-All)
- **Scripts renamed or deleted**
- **New dependency patterns** (e.g. a phase-e script now reads from phase-b's InventoryDataService)
- **Architecture refactor** (e.g. DataService split into two)

## Color palette for new phases (remeber background color in mind and make sure all assigned colors are visible too)

| Phase | Assigned Color |
|-------|---------------|
| All   | `#b89eff` (lavender) |
| A     | `#6cb4ff` (blue) |
| A-1   | `#7af0ff` (cyan) |
| B     | `#45eaad` (green) |
| C     | `#ffd04a` (yellow) |
| D     | `#ff8080` (red) |
| E     | `#ff9f43` (orange) — suggested |
| F     | `#a3e635` (lime) — suggested |
| G     | `#f0abfc` (magenta) — suggested |
| H     | `#67e8f9` (teal) — suggested |
| I     | `#fca5a5` (salmon) — suggested |
| J     | `#d4d4d8` (silver) — suggested |

    <div id="workspace">

        <!-- Raw -->
        <div class="panel on" id="panel-raw">
            <div id="raw-wrap">
                <div id="lnums"></div>
                <textarea id="raw-editor" spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" wrap="off"></textarea>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Preview -->
        <div class="panel" id="panel-preview">
            <div id="toc">
                <div id="toc-head"><span>Contents</span><button id="toc-close" title="Close sidebar">✕</button></div>
                <nav id="toc-nav"></nav>
            </div>
            <div id="prev-scroll">
                <article id="prev-body" class="md"></article>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Split -->
        <div class="panel" id="panel-split">
            <div id="split-raw">
                <div id="split-lnums"></div>
                <textarea id="split-editor" spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" wrap="off"></textarea>
            </div>
            <div id="vdivider"></div>
            <div id="split-prev-scroll">
                <article id="split-prev-body" class="md"></article>
            </div>
        </div>

    </div><!-- #workspace -->
</div><!-- #main -->

<!-- Status bar -->
<div id="sb">
    <div class="sp"><span class="l">Words</span><span class="v" id="sb-w">0</span></div>
    <div class="sp"><span class="l">Lines</span><span class="v" id="sb-l">0</span></div>
    <div class="sp"><span class="l">Chars</span><span class="v" id="sb-c">0</span></div>
    <div class="sp"><span class="l">Read</span><span class="v" id="sb-r">—</span></div>
    <div id="sb-spacer"></div>
    <div class="sp" style="border-right:none;border-left:1px solid rgba(52,211,153,.12)">
        <span class="l">Tab</span><span class="v" id="sb-tab">raw</span>
    </div>
</div>

</div><!-- #app -->

<!-- Hidden file input -->
<input type="file" id="file-in" accept=".md,.txt,.markdown" style="display:none" />

<!-- Toast -->
<div id="toast"></div>

<script>
/* ══ Utilities ══════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const esc = s => s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');

/* ══ State ══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
let MD = '';
let curTab   = localStorage.getItem('mdv_tab')   || 'raw';
let dark     = (localStorage.getItem('mdv_theme') || 'dark') === 'dark';
let fname    = 'untitled.md';
let currentFileId = null;   // stable id of the file currently open
let autoSaveTimer = null;
let renderPending = false;
let tocObserver = null;

// Apply persisted theme immediately (before paint)
document.documentElement.dataset.theme = dark ? 'dark' : 'light';

/* ══ Refs ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const landing      = $('landing');
const landCard     = $('land-card');
const landTA       = $('land-ta');
const workspace    = $('workspace');
const rawEditor    = $('raw-editor');
const splitEd      = $('split-editor');
const lnums        = $('lnums');
const splitLnums   = $('split-lnums');
const prevBody     = $('prev-body');
const splitPrev    = $('split-prev-body');
const tocEl        = $('toc');
const tocNav       = $('toc-nav');
const tabs         = $('tabs');
const pill         = $('tab-pill');

/* ══ marked.js renderer ═════════════════════════════════════ */
const renderer = new marked.Renderer();

// Headings → id + anchor
renderer.heading = function(text, level) {
    const slug = text
        .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '')   // strip any HTML tags from text
        .toLowerCase()
        .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '')
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
        .replace(/-+/g, '-')
        .trim();
    return `<h${level} id="${slug}">${text}<a class="h-link" href="#${slug}" aria-hidden="true">#</a></h${level}>\n`;
};

// Code fences → hljs + header bar
renderer.code = function(code, lang) {
    const raw = code.replace(/\t/g, '    ');
    const vl = lang && hljs.getLanguage(lang) ? lang : null;
    let hl;
    try { hl = vl ? hljs.highlight(raw, { language: vl }).value : hljs.highlightAuto(raw).value; }
    catch(e) { hl = esc(raw); }
    const badge = vl || (lang ? esc(lang) : 'text');
    const enc = encodeURIComponent(code);
    return `<pre><div class="code-hdr"><span class="lang-badge">${badge}</span><button class="ccopy" onclick="copyCode(this,'${enc}')">⎘ Copy</button></div><code class="hljs">${hl}</code></pre>\n`;
};

// Inline code
renderer.codespan = function(code) { return `<code>${code}</code>`; };

// Tables → scrollable wrapper
renderer.table = function(header, body) {
    return `<div class="tbl-wrap"><table><thead>${header}</thead><tbody>${body}</tbody></table></div>\n`;
};

// Images
renderer.image = function(href, title, text) {
    return `<img src="${esc(href)}" alt="${esc(text)}"${title ? ` title="${esc(title)}"` : ''} loading="lazy" />\n`;
};

// Links: external open in new tab
renderer.link = function(href, title, text) {
    if (!href) return text;
    const ext = !href.startsWith('#') && !href.startsWith('mailto:');
    return `<a href="${esc(href)}"${title ? ` title="${esc(title)}"` : ''}${ext ? ' target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"' : ''}>${text}</a>`;
};

// Blockquotes — detect GitHub-style callouts [!NOTE] etc.
renderer.blockquote = function(quote) {
    const types = { NOTE:'💬', TIP:'💡', WARNING:'⚠️', IMPORTANT:'❗', CAUTION:'🔥' };
    const m = quote.match(/<p>\[!(NOTE|TIP|WARNING|IMPORTANT|CAUTION)\](.*?)<\/p>/is);
    if (m) {
        const type = m[1].toUpperCase();
        const rest = m[2].trim();
        const body = quote
            .replace(/<p>\[!(NOTE|TIP|WARNING|IMPORTANT|CAUTION)\].*?<\/p>/is, rest ? `<p>${rest}</p>` : '');
        return `<blockquote data-callout="${type}"><p><strong>${types[type] || '📌'} ${type}</strong></p>${body}</blockquote>\n`;
    }
    return `<blockquote>${quote}</blockquote>\n`;
};

// Custom list items — handle task lists manually
renderer.listitem = function(text, task, checked) {
    if (task) {
        return `<li class="task-item"><input type="checkbox" class="task-cb"${checked ? ' checked' : ''} disabled />${text}</li>\n`;
    }
    return `<li>${text}</li>\n`;
};

marked.use({
    renderer,
    gfm: true,
    breaks: false,
    pedantic: false,
});

/* ══ Footnote pre-processing ════════════════════════════════ */
function processFootnotes(src) {
    const defs = {};
    const defRe = /^\[\^([^\]]+)\]:\s*(.+(?:\n(?!\s*\n).*)*)/gm;
    let m;
    while ((m = defRe.exec(src)) !== null) defs[m[1]] = m[2].trim();
    if (!Object.keys(defs).length) return src;

    const order = [];
    let out = src.replace(/\[\^([^\]]+)\](?!:)/g, (_, lbl) => {
        if (defs[lbl] === undefined) return `[^${lbl}]`;
        if (!order.includes(lbl)) order.push(lbl);
        const n = order.indexOf(lbl) + 1;
        return `<sup><a class="fn-ref" href="#fn-${lbl}" id="fnref-${lbl}">[${n}]</a></sup>`;
    });
    out = out.replace(/^\[\^[^\]]+\]:\s*.+$/gm, '');

    if (order.length) {
        let sec = '\n\n<div class="footnotes"><hr/><ol>';
        order.forEach(lbl => {
            sec += `<li class="fn-item" id="fn-${lbl}">${defs[lbl]} <a href="#fnref-${lbl}" class="fn-ref">↩</a></li>`;
        });
        sec += '</ol></div>';
        out += sec;
    }
    return out;
}

/* ══ Math-ish pre-processing (display $…$ as styled spans) ══ */
function processMath(src) {
    // Block math $$…$$
    src = src.replace(/\$\$([^$]+?)\$\$/gs, (_, inner) =>
        `<div class="math-block">${esc(inner.trim())}</div>`);
    // Inline math $…$
    src = src.replace(/\$([^$\n]+?)\$/g, (_, inner) =>
        `<span class="math-inline">${esc(inner.trim())}</span>`);
    return src;
}

/* ══ Main render ════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function renderMD(src) {
    let processed = processFootnotes(src);
    processed = processMath(processed);
    try { return marked.parse(processed); }
    catch(e) { return `<pre style="color:var(--red)">Parse error: ${esc(e.message)}</pre>`; }
}

function render() {
    const html = renderMD(MD);
    prevBody.innerHTML = html;
    splitPrev.innerHTML = html;
    buildTOC(html);
    updateStats();
}

function schedRender() {
    if (renderPending) return;
    renderPending = true;
    requestAnimationFrame(() => { renderPending = false; render(); });
}

/* ══ TOC ════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function buildTOC(html) {
    const tmp = document.createElement('div');
    tmp.innerHTML = html;
    const heads = tmp.querySelectorAll('h1[id],h2[id],h3[id],h4[id]');
    if (heads.length < 2) { tocEl.classList.remove('show'); return; }
    tocNav.innerHTML = '';
    heads.forEach(h => {
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.className = 'toc-a';
        a.href = '#' + h.id;
        a.dataset.id = h.id;
        a.dataset.lv = h.tagName[1];
        a.textContent = h.textContent.replace('#','').trim();
        a.addEventListener('click', e => {
            e.preventDefault();
            prevBody.parentElement.querySelector('#' + CSS.escape(h.id))?.scrollIntoView({ behavior:'smooth', block:'start' });
        });
        tocNav.appendChild(a);
    });
    if (!tocUserHidden) {
        tocEl.classList.add('show');
        $('btn-toc').style.color = 'var(--accent)';
        $('btn-toc').style.borderColor = 'var(--accent)';
    }
    setupTOCObserver();
}

function setupTOCObserver() {
    if (tocObserver) tocObserver.disconnect();
    const heads = prevBody.querySelectorAll('h1[id],h2[id],h3[id],h4[id]');
    if (!heads.length) return;
    tocObserver = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
        entries.forEach(e => {
            if (e.isIntersecting)
                tocNav.querySelectorAll('.toc-a').forEach(a =>
                    a.classList.toggle('active', a.dataset.id === e.target.id));
        });
    }, { root: $('prev-scroll'), rootMargin: '-10% 0px -80% 0px', threshold: 0 });
    heads.forEach(h => tocObserver.observe(h));
}

/* ══ Line numbers ════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function setLnums(src, el, curLine) {
    const n = src.split('\n').length;
    el.innerHTML = Array.from({ length: n }, (_, i) =>
        `<span class="ln${i + 1 === curLine ? ' cur' : ''}">${i + 1}</span>`
    ).join('');
}

function syncScroll(ta, nl) { nl.scrollTop = ta.scrollTop; }

/* ══ Stats ══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function updateStats() {
    const words = MD.trim() ? MD.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;
    const lines = MD.split('\n').length;
    const chars = MD.length;
    const mins  = Math.max(1, Math.round(words / 200));
    $('sb-w').textContent = words.toLocaleString();
    $('sb-l').textContent = lines.toLocaleString();
    $('sb-c').textContent = chars.toLocaleString();
    $('sb-r').textContent = `~${mins} min`;
}

/* ══ Tab switching ══════════════════════════════════════════ */
function setTab(tab) {
    curTab = tab;
    localStorage.setItem('mdv_tab', tab);
    document.querySelectorAll('.panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('on'));
    $('panel-' + tab).classList.add('on');
    document.querySelectorAll('.t-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('on', b.dataset.tab === tab));
    $('sb-tab').textContent = tab;

    // Move pill
    const btn = document.querySelector(`.t-btn[data-tab="${tab}"]`);
    if (btn) {
        const sr = tabs.getBoundingClientRect();
        const br = btn.getBoundingClientRect();
        pill.style.left  = (br.left - sr.left - 3) + 'px';
        pill.style.width = br.width + 'px';
    }

    if (tab !== 'raw') render();
    if (tab === 'split') {
        splitEd.value = MD;
        setLnums(MD, splitLnums);
    }
}

tabs.addEventListener('click', e => {
    const btn = e.target.closest('.t-btn');
    if (btn) setTab(btn.dataset.tab);
});

/* ══ Enter workspace ════════════════════════════════════════ */
function enter(src, name, existingId = null) {
    MD = src;
    fname = name || 'untitled.md';
    $('fname-display').value = fname;
    document.title = fname + ' — Markdown Viewer';
    rawEditor.value = MD;
    splitEd.value = MD;
    setLnums(MD, lnums);
    setLnums(MD, splitLnums);
    updateStats();
    landing.classList.add('hidden');
    workspace.classList.add('active');
    setTimeout(() => setTab(curTab), 40);
    // Always save/update history
    if (existingId) {
        currentFileId = existingId;
        updateCurrentInHistory(fname, src);
    } else {
        addToHistory(fname, src);
    }
}

/* ══ Landing actions ════════════════════════════════════════ */
$('btn-go').addEventListener('click', () => {
    enter(landTA.value || '', 'untitled.md');
    setTab('preview');
});

landTA.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); $('btn-go').click(); }
    if (e.key === 'Tab') {
        e.preventDefault();
        const s = landTA.selectionStart, f = landTA.selectionEnd;
        landTA.value = landTA.value.slice(0, s) + '    ' + landTA.value.slice(f);
        landTA.selectionStart = landTA.selectionEnd = s + 4;
    }
});

$('btn-open').addEventListener('click', () => $('file-in').click());

/* ══ File open ══════════════════════════════════════════════ */
$('file-in').addEventListener('change', e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0]; if (!file) return;
    const r = new FileReader();
    r.onload = ev => { enter(ev.target.result, file.name); setTab('preview'); };
    r.readAsText(file);
    e.target.value = '';
});

/* ══ Drag & drop ════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function drEv(el, enter, over, leave, drop) {
    el.addEventListener('dragenter',  enter);
    el.addEventListener('dragover',   over);
    el.addEventListener('dragleave',  leave);
    el.addEventListener('drop',       drop);
}

drEv(landCard,
    e => { e.preventDefault(); landCard.classList.add('drag-over'); },
    e => e.preventDefault(),
    e => { if (!landCard.contains(e.relatedTarget)) landCard.classList.remove('drag-over'); },
    e => {
        e.preventDefault(); landCard.classList.remove('drag-over');
        readDrop(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
    }
);

document.addEventListener('dragover', e => e.preventDefault());
document.addEventListener('drop', e => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const f = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
    if (f) readDrop(f);
});

function readDrop(file) {
    if (!file) return;
    const r = new FileReader();
    r.onload = ev => { enter(ev.target.result, file.name); setTab('preview'); };
    r.readAsText(file);
}

/* ══ Raw editor ═════════════════════════════════════════════ */
rawEditor.addEventListener('input', () => {
    MD = rawEditor.value;
    const cur = rawEditor.value.slice(0, rawEditor.selectionStart).split('\n').length;
    setLnums(MD, lnums, cur);
    schedRender();
    updateStats();
    schedAutoSave();
});
rawEditor.addEventListener('scroll', () => syncScroll(rawEditor, lnums));
rawEditor.addEventListener('keydown', editorKeys);
rawEditor.addEventListener('click', () => {
    const cur = rawEditor.value.slice(0, rawEditor.selectionStart).split('\n').length;
    setLnums(MD, lnums, cur);
});
rawEditor.addEventListener('keyup', () => {
    const cur = rawEditor.value.slice(0, rawEditor.selectionStart).split('\n').length;
    setLnums(MD, lnums, cur);
});

splitEd.addEventListener('input', () => {
    MD = splitEd.value;
    rawEditor.value = MD;
    setLnums(MD, splitLnums);
    schedRender();
    schedAutoSave();
});
splitEd.addEventListener('scroll', () => syncScroll(splitEd, splitLnums));
splitEd.addEventListener('keydown', editorKeys);

function editorKeys(e) {
    const ta = e.target;
    // Tab → 4 spaces
    if (e.key === 'Tab') {
        e.preventDefault();
        const s = ta.selectionStart, f = ta.selectionEnd;
        if (s === f) {
            ta.value = ta.value.slice(0,s) + '    ' + ta.value.slice(f);
            ta.selectionStart = ta.selectionEnd = s + 4;
        } else {
            // indent selection
            const lines = ta.value.split('\n');
            let cs = 0, seen = 0;
            const sel = { s, f };
            const out = lines.map(line => {
                const ls = cs, le = cs + line.length;
                cs = le + 1;
                if (ls <= sel.f && le >= sel.s) return '    ' + line;
                return line;
            });
            ta.value = out.join('\n');
        }
        MD = ta.value;
        rawEditor.value = MD; splitEd.value = MD;
        setLnums(MD, ta === rawEditor ? lnums : splitLnums);
        schedRender();
    }
    // Ctrl+Enter → preview
    if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); setTab('preview'); }
    // Auto-pairs
    const pairs = { '(':')', '[':']', '{':'}', '"':'"', "'":"'", '`':'`' };
    if (pairs[e.key]) {
        const s = ta.selectionStart, f = ta.selectionEnd;
        if (s !== f) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const sel = ta.value.slice(s, f);
            ta.value = ta.value.slice(0,s) + e.key + sel + pairs[e.key] + ta.value.slice(f);
            ta.selectionStart = s + 1; ta.selectionEnd = f + 1;
            MD = ta.value; rawEditor.value = MD; splitEd.value = MD;
            schedRender();
        }
    }
    // Enter in list item → continue list
    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        const s = ta.selectionStart;
        const lineStart = ta.value.lastIndexOf('\n', s - 1) + 1;
        const line = ta.value.slice(lineStart, s);
        const listMatch = line.match(/^(\s*)([-*+]|\d+\.)\s/);
        if (listMatch) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const prefix = listMatch[1] + listMatch[2] + ' ';
            ta.value = ta.value.slice(0, s) + '\n' + prefix + ta.value.slice(s);
            ta.selectionStart = ta.selectionEnd = s + 1 + prefix.length;
            MD = ta.value; rawEditor.value = MD; splitEd.value = MD;
            setLnums(MD, ta === rawEditor ? lnums : splitLnums);
            schedRender();
        }
    }
}

/* ══ Paste detection (landing) ══════════════════════════════ */
document.addEventListener('paste', e => {
    if (workspace.classList.contains('active')) return;
    if (document.activeElement === landTA) return;
    const t = e.clipboardData.getData('text/plain');
    if (t && t.trim()) { landTA.value = t; enter(t, 'pasted.md'); setTab('preview'); }
});

/* ══ Copy & Download ════════════════════════════════════════ */
async function doCopy(text) {
    try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); }
    catch {
        const ta = Object.assign(document.createElement('textarea'), { value: text });
        document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy'); ta.remove();
    }
}

$('btn-copy-md').addEventListener('click', async () => { await doCopy(MD); toast('✓ Markdown copied'); });
$('btn-copy-html').addEventListener('click', async () => {
    await doCopy(renderMD(MD)); toast('✓ HTML copied');
});
$('btn-dl').addEventListener('click', () => {
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([MD], { type:'text/markdown;charset=utf-8' }));
    a.download = fname.endsWith('.md') ? fname : fname + '.md';
    a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
});

// Code block copy button (called from inline HTML)
window.copyCode = async function(btn, enc) {
    await doCopy(decodeURIComponent(enc));
    btn.textContent = '✓ Copied'; btn.classList.add('ok');
    setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = '⎘ Copy'; btn.classList.remove('ok'); }, 1500);
};

/* ══ Logo → Home ════════════════════════════════════════════ */
$('logo').addEventListener('click', () => {
    clearTimeout(autoSaveTimer);
    if (currentFileId && MD.trim()) updateCurrentInHistory(fname, MD);
    workspace.classList.remove('active');
    landing.classList.remove('hidden');
    renderRecentList();
});

/* ══ Filename rename ════════════════════════════════════════ */
const fnameInput = $('fname-display');
fnameInput.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); fnameInput.blur(); }
    if (e.key === 'Escape') { fnameInput.value = fname; fnameInput.blur(); }
});
fnameInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
    let newName = fnameInput.value.trim() || 'untitled.md';
    if (!newName.match(/\.[a-zA-Z]+$/)) newName += '.md';
    const oldName = fname;
    fname = newName;
    fnameInput.value = fname;
    document.title = fname + ' — Markdown Viewer';
    // updateCurrentInHistory handles null currentFileId by calling addToHistory
    updateCurrentInHistory(fname, MD);
    if (newName !== oldName) toast('✓ Renamed → ' + fname);
});
// Prevent clicks on the filename field from bubbling to logo
fnameInput.addEventListener('click', e => e.stopPropagation());

/* ══ TOC toggle ═════════════════════════════════════════════ */
let tocUserHidden = localStorage.getItem('mdv_toc_hidden') === '1';

function setTocHidden(hide) {
    tocUserHidden = hide;
    localStorage.setItem('mdv_toc_hidden', hide ? '1' : '0');
    if (hide) {
        tocEl.classList.remove('show');
        $('btn-toc').style.color = '';
        $('btn-toc').style.borderColor = '';
    }
}

$('btn-toc').addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (tocEl.classList.contains('show')) {
        setTocHidden(true);
    } else {
        tocUserHidden = false;
        localStorage.setItem('mdv_toc_hidden', '0');
        tocEl.classList.add('show');
        $('btn-toc').style.color = 'var(--accent)';
        $('btn-toc').style.borderColor = 'var(--accent)';
    }
});

$('toc-close').addEventListener('click', () => setTocHidden(true));

/* ══ Preview width slider ════════════════════════════════════ */
const widthSlider = $('prev-width-slider');
const widthVal    = $('width-val');

function applyPreviewWidth(val) {
    const pct = val + '%';
    prevBody.style.maxWidth = pct;
    $('split-prev-body').style.maxWidth = pct;
    widthVal.textContent = val + '%';
}

(function() {
    const v = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('mdv_prev_width') || '72');
    widthSlider.value = v;
    applyPreviewWidth(v);
})();

widthSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
    applyPreviewWidth(parseInt(widthSlider.value));
    localStorage.setItem('mdv_prev_width', widthSlider.value);
});

/* ══ Font size slider ════════════════════════════════════════ */
const fontSlider = $('font-size-slider');
const fontSizeVal = $('font-size-val');

function applyFontSize(val) {
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--md-font-size', val + 'px');
    fontSizeVal.textContent = val + 'px';
}

(function() {
    const v = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('mdv_font_size') || '16');
    fontSlider.value = v;
    applyFontSize(v);
})();

fontSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
    applyFontSize(parseInt(fontSlider.value));
    localStorage.setItem('mdv_font_size', fontSlider.value);
});

/* ══ localStorage history ═══════════════════════════════════ */
const HIST_KEY = 'mdv_history';
const HIST_MAX = 40;

function loadHistory() {
    try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(HIST_KEY) || '[]'); }
    catch { return []; }
}
function saveHistoryArr(arr) {
    localStorage.setItem(HIST_KEY, JSON.stringify(arr.slice(0, HIST_MAX)));
}
function genId() {
    return Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);
}

// Always creates a brand-new entry (new paste / new file drop).
// Does NOT deduplicate by name — same-name files coexist.
function addToHistory(name, content) {
    const id = genId();
    const hist = loadHistory();
    hist.unshift({ id, name, content, ts: Date.now() });
    saveHistoryArr(hist);
    currentFileId = id;
    renderRecentList();
}

// Updates an existing entry by its stable id.
// If the id is missing (edge case), falls back to addToHistory.
function updateCurrentInHistory(newName, newContent) {
    if (!currentFileId) {
        // No id yet — create a fresh entry now
        addToHistory(newName, newContent);
        return;
    }
    const hist = loadHistory();
    const idx  = hist.findIndex(h => h.id === currentFileId);
    if (idx === -1) { addToHistory(newName, newContent); return; }
    const entry = { ...hist[idx], name: newName, content: newContent, ts: Date.now() };
    hist.splice(idx, 1);
    hist.unshift(entry);
    saveHistoryArr(hist);
    renderRecentList();
}

function schedAutoSave() {
    clearTimeout(autoSaveTimer);
    autoSaveTimer = setTimeout(() => updateCurrentInHistory(fname, MD), 1800);
}

function formatRelTime(ts) {
    const diff = Date.now() - ts;
    const m = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
    const h = Math.floor(m / 60);
    const d = Math.floor(h / 24);
    if (d > 0) return `${d}d ago`;
    if (h > 0) return `${h}h ago`;
    if (m > 0) return `${m}m ago`;
    return 'just now';
}

let recentSearchQ = '';

function renderRecentList() {
    const allHist = loadHistory();
    const sec  = $('recent-section');
    const list = $('recent-list');
    const q    = recentSearchQ.toLowerCase().trim();
    const hist = q ? allHist.filter(h => h.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                                         h.content.toLowerCase().includes(q)) : allHist;

    if (!allHist.length) { sec.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    sec.style.display = '';
    list.innerHTML = '';

    if (!hist.length) {
        list.innerHTML = `<div id="recent-empty">No files match "${esc(q)}"</div>`;
        return;
    }

    hist.forEach(item => {
        // Build body preview: show raw markdown lines (like a code file card)
        const bodyLines = item.content.split('\n').slice(0, 8).join('\n').slice(0, 400);
        const wordCount = item.content.trim() ? item.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;

        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'rc';
        card.dataset.id = item.id;
        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="rc-hdr">
                <span class="rc-icon">📄</span>
                <span class="rc-name" contenteditable="false" spellcheck="false" title="Double-click to rename">${esc(item.name)}</span>
                <div class="rc-meta">
                    <span>${formatRelTime(item.ts)}</span>
                    <span class="rc-meta-dot">·</span>
                    <span>${wordCount.toLocaleString()}w</span>
                    <span class="rc-meta-dot">·</span>
                    <span>${(item.content.length / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB</span>
                    ${item.fromUrl ? '<span class="rc-tag">url</span>' : ''}
                </div>
                <button class="rc-del" title="Delete">✕</button>
            </div>
            <div class="rc-body">${esc(bodyLines) || '<span style="opacity:.4">Empty file</span>'}</div>`;

        const nameEl = card.querySelector('.rc-name');
        const delBtn = card.querySelector('.rc-del');

        // Open file on click (not when editing name or deleting)
        card.addEventListener('click', e => {
            if (e.target === delBtn || nameEl.contentEditable === 'true') return;
            enter(item.content, item.name, item.id);
            setTab(curTab);
        });

        // Double-click name to rename inline
        nameEl.addEventListener('dblclick', e => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            nameEl.contentEditable = 'true';
            nameEl.focus();
            const range = document.createRange();
            range.selectNodeContents(nameEl);
            window.getSelection().removeAllRanges();
            window.getSelection().addRange(range);
        });
        nameEl.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); nameEl.blur(); }
            if (e.key === 'Escape') { nameEl.textContent = esc(item.name); nameEl.blur(); }
            e.stopPropagation();
        });
        nameEl.addEventListener('blur', () => {
            nameEl.contentEditable = 'false';
            let newName = nameEl.textContent.trim() || item.name;
            if (!newName.match(/\.[a-zA-Z]+$/)) newName += '.md';
            nameEl.textContent = newName;
            // Update this specific entry in history by id
            const hist2 = loadHistory();
            const i2 = hist2.findIndex(h => h.id === item.id);
            if (i2 !== -1) {
                hist2[i2].name = newName;
                saveHistoryArr(hist2);
                item.name = newName; // update local ref
                // If this is the currently open file, sync header too
                if (item.id === currentFileId) {
                    fname = newName;
                    $('fname-display').value = newName;
                    document.title = newName + ' — Markdown Viewer';
                }
            }
            renderRecentList();
        });

        // Delete
        delBtn.addEventListener('click', e => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            const hist2 = loadHistory().filter(h => h.id !== item.id);
            saveHistoryArr(hist2);
            if (item.id === currentFileId) currentFileId = null;
            renderRecentList();
        });

        list.appendChild(card);
    });
}

// Search filter
$('recent-search').addEventListener('input', e => {
    recentSearchQ = e.target.value;
    renderRecentList();
});
// Clear all
$('recent-clear').addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (!confirm('Clear all file history? This cannot be undone.')) return;
    localStorage.removeItem(HIST_KEY);
    currentFileId = null;
    renderRecentList();
});

// Render on page load
renderRecentList();

/* ══ URL hash — load shared file ════════════════════════════ */
(function() {
    const hash = location.hash.slice(1);
    if (!hash || hash.length < 8) return;
    try {
        const content = LZString.decompressFromBase64(hash);
        if (content && content.length > 0) {
            // Clear hash from URL without reload
            history.replaceState(null, '', location.pathname + location.search);
            // Enter with a generated name
            const nameFromHash = 'fromurl.md';
            // Small delay so DOM is ready
            setTimeout(() => {
                enter(content, nameFromHash);
                // Mark as fromUrl in history
                const hist = loadHistory();
                const idx  = hist.findIndex(h => h.id === currentFileId);
                if (idx !== -1) { hist[idx].fromUrl = true; saveHistoryArr(hist); }
                setTab('preview');
                toast('📎 Loaded from shared link');
            }, 80);
        }
    } catch(e) { /* Not a valid hash — ignore */ }
})();

/* ══ Share link ══════════════════════════════════════════════ */
$('btn-share').addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (!MD.trim()) { toast('⚠ Nothing to share'); return; }
    const compressed = LZString.compressToBase64(MD);
    const url = location.origin + location.pathname + '#' + compressed;
    try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url); }
    catch {
        const ta = Object.assign(document.createElement('textarea'), { value: url });
        document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy'); ta.remove();
    }
    toast('🔗 Share link copied!', 2400);
});

/* ══ Theme toggle ═══════════════════════════════════════════ */
$('btn-theme').addEventListener('click', () => {
    dark = !dark;
    document.documentElement.dataset.theme = dark ? 'dark' : 'light';
    $('btn-theme').textContent = dark ? '🌙' : '☀️';
    localStorage.setItem('mdv_theme', dark ? 'dark' : 'light');
});
$('btn-theme').textContent = dark ? '🌙' : '☀️';

/* ══ Toast ══════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function toast(msg, dur = 1800) {
    const t = $('toast'); t.textContent = msg;
    t.classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), dur);
}

/* ══ Split divider drag (with saved position) ═══════════════ */
(function() {
    const div = $('vdivider'), sr = $('split-raw'), sp = $('split-prev-scroll');
    let drag = false;
    // Restore saved split
    const savedSplit = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('mdv_split_pct') || '50');
    sr.style.flex = `0 0 ${savedSplit}%`;
    sp.style.flex  = `0 0 ${100 - savedSplit}%`;

    div.addEventListener('mousedown', () => {
        drag = true; div.classList.add('drag');
        document.body.style.cssText += 'cursor:col-resize;user-select:none';
    });
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
        if (!drag) return;
        const p = div.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
        const pct = Math.max(20, Math.min(80, (e.clientX - p.left) / p.width * 100));
        sr.style.flex = `0 0 ${pct}%`;
        sp.style.flex  = `0 0 ${100 - pct}%`;
    });
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        if (!drag) return;
        drag = false; div.classList.remove('drag');
        document.body.style.cursor = ''; document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        // Save position
        const curPct = parseFloat(sr.style.flex.match(/[\d.]+/)?.[0] || 50);
        localStorage.setItem('mdv_split_pct', Math.round(curPct));
    });
})();

/* ══ Pill init ══════════════════════════════════════════════ */
window.addEventListener('load', () => {
    hljs.configure({ tabReplace: '    ' });
    document.querySelectorAll('.t-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('on', b.dataset.tab === curTab));
    const b = document.querySelector('.t-btn.on');
    if (b) {
        const sr = tabs.getBoundingClientRect(), br = b.getBoundingClientRect();
        pill.style.left = (br.left - sr.left - 3) + 'px';
        pill.style.width = br.width + 'px';
    }
});
</script>
</body>

  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'BuildingDataService', type:'creates', label:'new BuildingDataService()' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'BuildingObject', type:'get', label:'ghost instantiate + fields' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'BuildingPlacementNode', type:'get', label:'.All static list' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'UtilsPhaseD', type:'uses-util', label:'IsOverlapping/IsFlatGround' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'UtilsPhaseB', type:'uses-util', label:'SetLayerRecursively' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'BuildingCrate', type:'get', label:'_buildingCratePrefab' },
  { source:'BuildingManager', target:'ToolBuilder', type:'get', label:'_buildingToolPrefab' },
  { source:'BuildingDataService', target:'BuildingObject', type:'get', label:'SnapPositions lists' },
  { source:'BuildingDataService', target:'BuildingRotationInfo', type:'get', label:'constructor + resolve' },
  { source:'ConveyorBeltManager', target:'BasePhysicsObject', type:'get', label:'SumVelocity/Count/Rb' },
  { source:'ConveyorBeltManager', target:'ConveyorBelt', type:'get', label:'AllConveyorBelts/ClearNull' },
  { source:'ConveyorBelt', target:'BasePhysicsObject', type:'set', label:'AddConveyorVelocity()' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'SO_BuildingInvDef', type:'get', label:'_definition fields' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'SO_InteractionOption', type:'get', label:'interactionType field' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'BaseModularSupports', type:'get', label:'RespawnSupports()' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'ModularBuildingSupports', type:'get', label:'RespawnSupports()' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'GlobalEnumsB', type:'get', label:'InteractionType.Take' },
  { source:'BuildingCrate', target:'SO_BuildingInvDef', type:'get', label:'definition fields' },
  { source:'BuildingCrate', target:'SO_InteractionOption', type:'get', label:'interactionType field' },
  { source:'BuildingCrate', target:'EconomyManager', type:'singleton', label:'Ins.GetMoney' },
  { source:'BuildingCrate', target:'GlobalEnumsB', type:'get', label:'InteractionType.Take/Destroy' },

  // ── SET/WRITE DEPENDENCIES ──
  { source:'PlayerGrab', target:'BaseHeldTool', type:'set', label:'SetOwner(movement)' },
  { source:'OrePiece', target:'UtilsPhaseAll', type:'uses-util', label:'SetTag()' },
  { source:'DamageableOrePiece', target:'UtilsPhaseB', type:'uses-util', label:'SimpleExplosion' },
  { source:'PlayerGrab', target:'UtilsPhaseB', type:'uses-util', label:'IgnoreAllCollisions' },
  { source:'BuildingObject', target:'UtilsPhaseB', type:'uses-util', label:'SetLayerRecursively' },
];

// count edges per node for radius scaling
links.forEach(l => {
  const s = nodes.find(n => n.id === l.source);
  const t = nodes.find(n => n.id === l.target);
  if (s) s.edgeCount = (s.edgeCount||0) + 1;
  if (t) t.edgeCount = (t.edgeCount||0) + 1;
});
nodes.forEach(n => { n.radius = Math.max(6, Math.min(18, 5 + (n.edgeCount||0) * 0.8)); });

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// D3 FORCE GRAPH
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const W = window.innerWidth, H = window.innerHeight;
const svg = d3.select('#graph').attr('viewBox', [0,0,W,H]);
const defs = svg.append('defs');

// arrow markers per edge type
const edgeTypes = ['inherit','interface','get','set','event-sub','event-raise','singleton','creates','uses-util'];
const edgeColors = { inherit:'#a78bfa', interface:'#67e8f9', get:'#34d399', set:'#f87171', 'event-sub':'#fbbf24', 'event-raise':'#fb923c', singleton:'#c084fc', creates:'#f472b6', 'uses-util':'#94a3b8' };
edgeTypes.forEach(t => {
  defs.append('marker').attr('id', 'arrow-'+t).attr('viewBox','0 -5 10 10')
    .attr('refX',22).attr('refY',0).attr('markerWidth',6).attr('markerHeight',6).attr('orient','auto')
    .append('path').attr('d','M0,-5L10,0L0,5').attr('fill', edgeColors[t]);
});

const g = svg.append('g');
const zoom = d3.zoom().scaleExtent([0.15, 4]).on('zoom', e => g.attr('transform', e.transform));
svg.call(zoom);

const simulation = d3.forceSimulation(nodes)
  .force('link', d3.forceLink(links).id(d => d.id).distance(d => {
    if (d.type === 'inherit') return 60;
    if (d.type === 'interface') return 80;
    return 100;
  }).strength(d => {
    if (d.type === 'inherit') return 0.8;
    if (d.type === 'interface') return 0.3;
    return 0.15;
  }))
  .force('charge', d3.forceManyBody().strength(-300).distanceMax(500))
  .force('center', d3.forceCenter(W/2, H/2))
  .force('collision', d3.forceCollide().radius(d => d.radius + 12))
  .force('x', d3.forceX(W/2).strength(0.03))
  .force('y', d3.forceY(H/2).strength(0.03));

const linkG = g.append('g').attr('class','links');
const nodeG = g.append('g').attr('class','nodes');

const link = linkG.selectAll('path.link')
  .data(links).join('path')
  .attr('class', d => 'link ' + d.type)
  .attr('marker-end', d => 'url(#arrow-' + d.type + ')')
  .attr('stroke', d => edgeColors[d.type]);

const node = nodeG.selectAll('g.node')
  .data(nodes).join('g')
  .attr('class','node')
  .call(d3.drag()
    .on('start', (e,d) => { if (!e.active) simulation.alphaTarget(0.3).restart(); d.fx=d.x; d.fy=d.y; })
    .on('drag', (e,d) => { d.fx=e.x; d.fy=e.y; })
    .on('end', (e,d) => { if (!e.active) simulation.alphaTarget(0); d.fx=null; d.fy=null; })
  );

node.append('circle')
  .attr('r', d => d.radius)
  .attr('fill', d => PHASE_COLORS[d.phase])
  .attr('stroke', d => d3.color(PHASE_COLORS[d.phase]).brighter(0.5))
  .attr('opacity', 0.85);

node.append('text')
  .attr('dx', d => d.radius + 4)
  .attr('dy', 3)
  .text(d => d.label);

// tooltip on hover
node.append('title').text(d => `${d.label}\n${d.phase.toUpperCase()} / ${layerLabel(d.layer)}\n${d.type}\nConnections: ${d.edgeCount}`);

simulation.on('tick', () => {
  link.attr('d', d => {
    const dx = d.target.x - d.source.x, dy = d.target.y - d.source.y;
    const dr = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy) * 1.5;
    return `M${d.source.x},${d.source.y}A${dr},${dr} 0 0,1 ${d.target.x},${d.target.y}`;
  });
  node.attr('transform', d => `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`);
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CONTROLS: phase toggles
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const phaseNames = { all:'Phase-All', a:'Phase-A', a1:'Phase-A1', b:'Phase-B', c:'Phase-C', d:'Phase-D' };
const activePhases = new Set(Object.keys(phaseNames));
const activeEdges = new Set(edgeTypes);

const phaseContainer = document.getElementById('phase-toggles');
Object.entries(phaseNames).forEach(([key, name]) => {
  const btn = document.createElement('button');
  btn.className = `ctrl-btn phase-${key} active`;
  btn.textContent = name;
  btn.onclick = () => {
    if (activePhases.has(key)) activePhases.delete(key); else activePhases.add(key);
    btn.classList.toggle('active');
    updateVisibility();
  };
  phaseContainer.appendChild(btn);
});

const edgeContainer = document.getElementById('edge-toggles');
edgeTypes.forEach(t => {
  const btn = document.createElement('button');
  btn.className = 'ctrl-btn active';
  btn.textContent = t;
  btn.style.borderLeftColor = edgeColors[t];
  btn.style.borderLeftWidth = '3px';
  btn.style.borderLeftStyle = 'solid';
  btn.onclick = () => {
    if (activeEdges.has(t)) activeEdges.delete(t); else activeEdges.add(t);
    btn.classList.toggle('active');
    updateVisibility();
  };
  edgeContainer.appendChild(btn);
});

function updateVisibility() {
  node.style('display', d => activePhases.has(d.phase) ? null : 'none');
  link.style('display', d => {
    const sVis = activePhases.has(d.source.phase);
    const tVis = activePhases.has(d.target.phase);
    return (sVis && tVis && activeEdges.has(d.type)) ? null : 'none';
  });
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// HIGHLIGHT on click
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let selectedNode = null;
node.on('click', (e, d) => {
  e.stopPropagation();
  if (selectedNode === d) { clearHighlight(); selectedNode = null; return; }
  selectedNode = d;
  highlight(d);
  showInfo(d);
});
svg.on('click', () => { clearHighlight(); selectedNode = null; document.getElementById('info-panel').style.display='none'; });

function highlight(d) {
  const connected = new Set();
  connected.add(d.id);
  links.forEach(l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    if (sid === d.id) connected.add(tid);
    if (tid === d.id) connected.add(sid);
  });
  node.classed('dimmed', n => !connected.has(n.id));
  node.classed('highlighted', n => n.id === d.id);
  link.classed('dimmed', l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    return !(sid === d.id || tid === d.id);
  });
  link.classed('highlighted', l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    return (sid === d.id || tid === d.id);
  });
}
function clearHighlight() {
  node.classed('dimmed', false).classed('highlighted', false);
  link.classed('dimmed', false).classed('highlighted', false);
}

function showInfo(d) {
  const panel = document.getElementById('info-panel');
  panel.style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('info-name').textContent = d.label;
  document.getElementById('info-phase').textContent = `Phase: ${phaseNames[d.phase]} · Layer: ${layerLabel(d.layer)}`;
  document.getElementById('info-type').textContent = `Type: ${d.type} · Connections: ${d.edgeCount}`;
  const depDiv = document.getElementById('info-deps');
  depDiv.innerHTML = '';
  links.forEach(l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    if (sid === d.id) {
      const target = nodes.find(n => n.id === tid);
      depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="dep-item"><span class="dep-dir">→</span> ${target?.label || tid} <span class="dep-type">[${l.type}]${l.label ? ' ' + l.label : ''}</span></div>`;
    }
    if (tid === d.id) {
      const source = nodes.find(n => n.id === sid);
      depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="dep-item"><span class="dep-dir">←</span> ${source?.label || sid} <span class="dep-type">[${l.type}]${l.label ? ' ' + l.label : ''}</span></div>`;
    }
  });
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SEARCH
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
document.getElementById('search').addEventListener('input', e => {
  const q = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
  if (!q) { clearHighlight(); return; }
  const matches = nodes.filter(n => n.label.toLowerCase().includes(q) || n.id.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  if (matches.length === 0) { clearHighlight(); return; }
  const matchIds = new Set(matches.map(n => n.id));
  const connected = new Set(matchIds);
  links.forEach(l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    if (matchIds.has(sid)) connected.add(tid);
    if (matchIds.has(tid)) connected.add(sid);
  });
  node.classed('dimmed', n => !connected.has(n.id));
  node.classed('highlighted', n => matchIds.has(n.id));
  link.classed('dimmed', l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    return !(matchIds.has(sid) || matchIds.has(tid));
  });
  link.classed('highlighted', l => {
    const sid = typeof l.source === 'object' ? l.source.id : l.source;
    const tid = typeof l.target === 'object' ? l.target.id : l.target;
    return (matchIds.has(sid) || matchIds.has(tid));
  });
});

// initial zoom to fit
svg.call(zoom.transform, d3.zoomIdentity.translate(W*0.1, H*0.1).scale(0.8));
</script>
</body>
</html>

<div id="legend">
  <div class="leg-col">
    <h4>Phases</h4>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-all)"></div>All</div>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-a)"></div>A</div>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-a1)"></div>A-1</div>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-b)"></div>B</div>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-c)"></div>C</div>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-dot" style="background:var(--phase-d)"></div>D</div>
  </div>
  <div class="leg-col">
    <h4>Edges</h4>
    <div class="leg-item"><div class="leg-line" style="border-color:var(--edge-inherit)"></div>Inherits</div>

  {s:'OrePoolMgr',t:'OrePieceKey',type:'get',lbl:'lookup key'},
  {s:'OrePoolMgr',t:'BasePhysObj',type:'get',lbl:'STANDARD_DAMPING'},
  {s:'OrePoolMgr',t:'UtilsAll',type:'uses-util',lbl:'SetTag()'},
  {s:'OrePoolMgr',t:'IEnumUtils',type:'uses-util',lbl:'GetOrCreate()'},
  {s:'OreNode',t:'UtilsC',type:'uses-util',lbl:'WeightedRandom()'},{s:'OreNode',t:'WNodeDrop',type:'get',lbl:'_possibleDrops'},
  {s:'AutoMiner',t:'SO_AutoMinerDef',type:'get',lbl:'SpawnProb/Rate/Prefabs'},{s:'AutoMiner',t:'UtilsC',type:'uses-util',lbl:'PickOrePrefab()'},
  {s:'SellerMachine',t:'OrePiece',type:'get',lbl:'SellAfterDelay()'},
  {s:'SellerMachine',t:'BaseSellable',type:'get',lbl:'GetSellValue()'},
  {s:'SellerMachine',t:'UtilsAll',type:'uses-util',lbl:'HasTag()'},
  {s:'UtilsC',t:'IEnumUtils',type:'uses-util',lbl:'.sum()'},
  {s:'UtilsC',t:'WOreChance',type:'get',lbl:'WeightedRandom list'},
  {s:'OreDataService',t:'ResourceDesc',type:'get',lbl:'descriptions'},{s:'OreDataService',t:'GlobalEnumsC',type:'get',lbl:'ResourceType'},
  {s:'PhaseALOG',t:'ShopDataService',type:'get',lbl:'CartItem fields'},
  {s:'UtilsA',t:'ShopSpawnPoint',type:'get',lbl:'GetRandomSpawnPoint()'},
  {s:'UtilsA',t:'SO_ShopItemDef',type:'get',lbl:'pfObject'},
  {s:'ShopDataService',t:'SO_ShopCategory',type:'get',lbl:'ITEM_DEF'},{s:'ShopDataService',t:'SO_ShopItemDef',type:'get',lbl:'price/locked'},
  {s:'ShopUITest',t:'ShopUI',type:'get',lbl:'GetDataServiceForTest()'},
  {s:'ElevatorTest',t:'StartingElevator',type:'get',lbl:'_elevator ref'},{s:'ElevatorTest',t:'CameraShaker',type:'get',lbl:'ApplyViewPunch()'},
  {s:'StartingElevator',t:'SimplePlayerCtrl',type:'get',lbl:'FindObjectOfType'},
  {s:'BuildingMgr',t:'BuildDataSvc',type:'creates',lbl:'new BuildDataSvc()'},
  {s:'BuildingMgr',t:'BuildingObj',type:'get',lbl:'ghost/fields'},
  {s:'BuildingMgr',t:'BuildPlaceNode',type:'get',lbl:'.All list'},
  {s:'BuildingMgr',t:'UtilsD',type:'uses-util',lbl:'IsOverlapping'},{s:'BuildingMgr',t:'UtilsB',type:'uses-util',lbl:'SetLayerRecursively'},
  {s:'BuildDataSvc',t:'BuildingObj',type:'get',lbl:'SnapPositions'},{s:'BuildDataSvc',t:'BuildRotInfo',type:'get',lbl:'constructor'},
  {s:'ConveyorMgr',t:'BasePhysObj',type:'get',lbl:'SumVelocity/Count'},
  {s:'ConveyorMgr',t:'ConveyorBelt',type:'get',lbl:'AllBelts/ClearNull'},
  {s:'ConveyorBelt',t:'BasePhysObj',type:'set',lbl:'AddConveyorVelocity'},
  {s:'BuildingObj',t:'SO_BuildInvDef',type:'get',lbl:'definition'},{s:'BuildingObj',t:'BaseModSupp',type:'get',lbl:'RespawnSupports'},
  {s:'BuildingObj',t:'GlobalEnumsB',type:'get',lbl:'InteractionType.Take'},
  {s:'BuildingCrate',t:'SO_BuildInvDef',type:'get',lbl:'definition'},
  {s:'BuildingCrate',t:'GlobalEnumsB',type:'get',lbl:'InteractionType'},
  // SET / WRITES
  {s:'PlayerGrab',t:'BaseHeldTool',type:'set',lbl:'SetOwner(movement)'},
  {s:'DmgOrePiece',t:'UtilsB',type:'uses-util',lbl:'SimpleExplosion'},
  {s:'PlayerGrab',t:'UtilsB',type:'uses-util',lbl:'IgnoreAllCollisions'},
  {s:'BuildingObj',t:'UtilsB',type:'uses-util',lbl:'SetLayerRecursively'},
  {s:'OrePiece',t:'UtilsAll',type:'uses-util',lbl:'SetTag()'},
];

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// GRID LAYOUT: compute positions
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// Group nodes into cells
const cells = {};
nodes.forEach(n => {
  const key = n.phase + '|' + n.layer;
  if (!cells[key]) cells[key] = [];
  cells[key].push(n);
});

// Compute max cell height per row
const rowMaxCounts = {};
LAYERS.forEach(layer => {
  let mx = 0;
  PHASES.forEach(phase => {
    const key = phase + '|' + layer;
    mx = Math.max(mx, (cells[key]||[]).length);
  });
  rowMaxCounts[layer] = mx;
});

// Compute row Y positions (variable height rows)
const rowY = {};
let cumY = MARGIN.top;
LAYERS.forEach(layer => {
  rowY[layer] = cumY;
  const cnt = Math.max(rowMaxCounts[layer], 1);
  cumY += Math.max(ROW_H, cnt * (NODE_H + NODE_PAD) + 50);
});
const totalH = cumY + MARGIN.bottom;

// Column X positions
const colX = {};
PHASES.forEach((phase, i) => { colX[phase] = MARGIN.left + i * COL_W; });
const totalW = MARGIN.left + PHASES.length * COL_W + MARGIN.right;

// Assign node positions
nodes.forEach(n => {
  const key = n.phase + '|' + n.layer;
  const cellNodes = cells[key];
  const idx = cellNodes.indexOf(n);
  n.x = colX[n.phase] + 20;
  n.y = rowY[n.layer] + 30 + idx * (NODE_H + NODE_PAD);
  n.cx = n.x + NODE_W / 2;
  n.cy = n.y + NODE_H / 2;
});

// Build node lookup
const nodeMap = {};
nodes.forEach(n => { nodeMap[n.id] = n; });

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RENDER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const svg = d3.select('#svg');
const g = svg.append('g');
const zoom = d3.zoom().scaleExtent([0.2, 3]).on('zoom', e => g.attr('transform', e.transform));
svg.call(zoom);

// Draw phase column backgrounds + headers
const colBgG = g.append('g').attr('class','col-bgs');
PHASES.forEach((phase, i) => {
  const x = colX[phase] - 10;
  colBgG.append('rect').attr('class','phase-col-bg')
    .attr('x', x).attr('y', MARGIN.top - 30).attr('width', COL_W - 10).attr('height', totalH - MARGIN.top)
    .attr('fill', PHASE_COLORS[phase]);
  colBgG.append('text').attr('class','phase-col-header')
    .attr('x', x + (COL_W - 10)/2).attr('y', MARGIN.top - 12)
    .text(PHASE_LABELS[phase]).attr('fill', PHASE_COLORS[phase]);
});

// Draw layer row lines + headers
const rowG = g.append('g').attr('class','row-lines');
LAYERS.forEach(layer => {
  const y = rowY[layer];
  rowG.append('line').attr('class','layer-row-line')
    .attr('x1', MARGIN.left - 20).attr('y1', y)
    .attr('x2', totalW).attr('y2', y);
  rowG.append('text').attr('class','layer-row-header')
    .attr('x', MARGIN.left - 25).attr('y', y + 16)
    .text(LAYER_LABELS[layer]);
});

// Arrow markers
const defs = svg.append('defs');
EDGE_TYPES.forEach(t => {
  defs.append('marker').attr('id','a-'+t).attr('viewBox','0 -4 8 8')
    .attr('refX',8).attr('refY',0).attr('markerWidth',5).attr('markerHeight',5).attr('orient','auto')
    .append('path').attr('d','M0,-4L8,0L0,4').attr('fill', EDGE_COLORS[t]);
});

// Draw edges
const edgeG = g.append('g').attr('class','edges');
const edgeEls = edgeG.selectAll('path.edge')
  .data(links.filter(l => nodeMap[l.s] && nodeMap[l.t]))
  .join('path')
  .attr('class', d => 'edge ' + d.type)
  .attr('marker-end', d => 'url(#a-' + d.type + ')')
  .attr('stroke', d => EDGE_COLORS[d.type])
  .each(function(d) {
    const src = nodeMap[d.s], tgt = nodeMap[d.t];
    if (!src || !tgt) return;
    // Determine connection points on node rects
    let sx, sy, tx, ty;
    if (src.x + NODE_W < tgt.x) { // src left of target
      sx = src.x + NODE_W; sy = src.cy; tx = tgt.x; ty = tgt.cy;
    } else if (tgt.x + NODE_W < src.x) { // src right of target
      sx = src.x; sy = src.cy; tx = tgt.x + NODE_W; ty = tgt.cy;
    } else if (src.y < tgt.y) { // src above target
      sx = src.cx; sy = src.y + NODE_H; tx = tgt.cx; ty = tgt.y;
    } else { // src below target
      sx = src.cx; sy = src.y; tx = tgt.cx; ty = tgt.y + NODE_H;
    }
    // Cubic bezier with gentle curve
    const dx = tx - sx, dy = ty - sy;
    const mx = (sx + tx) / 2, my = (sy + ty) / 2;
    let cx1, cy1, cx2, cy2;
    if (Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
      cx1 = sx + dx * 0.3; cy1 = sy;
      cx2 = tx - dx * 0.3; cy2 = ty;
    } else {
      cx1 = sx; cy1 = sy + dy * 0.3;
      cx2 = tx; cy2 = ty - dy * 0.3;
    }
    d3.select(this).attr('d', `M${sx},${sy} C${cx1},${cy1} ${cx2},${cy2} ${tx},${ty}`);
  });

// Draw nodes
const nodeG = g.append('g').attr('class','nodes');
const nodeEls = nodeG.selectAll('g.node')
  .data(nodes).join('g')
  .attr('class','node')
  .attr('transform', d => `translate(${d.x},${d.y})`);

nodeEls.append('rect')
  .attr('width', NODE_W).attr('height', NODE_H)
  .attr('fill', d => {
    const c = d3.color(PHASE_COLORS[d.phase]);
    c.opacity = 0.15;
    return c + '';
  })
  .attr('stroke', d => PHASE_COLORS[d.phase])
  .attr('opacity', 0.9);

nodeEls.append('text')
  .attr('x', 5).attr('y', NODE_H / 2 - 3)
  .text(d => d.label);

nodeEls.append('text')
  .attr('class','type-label')
  .attr('x', 5).attr('y', NODE_H / 2 + 8)
  .text(d => d.type);

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// INTERACTIONS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// Edge toggle bar
const edgeBar = document.getElementById('edge-bar');
EDGE_TYPES.forEach(t => {
  const btn = document.createElement('button');
  btn.className = 'edge-btn active';
  btn.innerHTML = `<span class="edge-swatch" style="background:${EDGE_COLORS[t]}"></span>${EDGE_LABELS[t]}`;
  btn.onclick = () => {
    if (activeEdges.has(t)) { activeEdges.delete(t); btn.classList.add('off'); btn.classList.remove('active'); }
    else { activeEdges.add(t); btn.classList.remove('off'); btn.classList.add('active'); }
    edgeEls.style('display', d => activeEdges.has(d.type) ? null : 'none');
  };
  edgeBar.appendChild(btn);
});

// Click node to highlight + show info
let selectedId = null;
nodeEls.on('click', (e, d) => {
  e.stopPropagation();
  if (selectedId === d.id) { clearHL(); return; }
  selectedId = d.id;
  highlightNode(d);
  showInfo(d);
});
svg.on('click', () => clearHL());

function highlightNode(d) {
  const connected = new Set([d.id]);
  links.forEach(l => {
    if (l.s === d.id) connected.add(l.t);
    if (l.t === d.id) connected.add(l.s);
  });
  nodeEls.classed('dimmed', n => !connected.has(n.id));
  nodeEls.classed('highlighted', n => n.id === d.id);
  edgeEls.classed('dimmed', l => !(l.s === d.id || l.t === d.id));
  edgeEls.classed('highlighted', l => (l.s === d.id || l.t === d.id));
}

function clearHL() {
  selectedId = null;
  nodeEls.classed('dimmed', false).classed('highlighted', false);
  edgeEls.classed('dimmed', false).classed('highlighted', false);
  document.getElementById('info').style.display = 'none';
}

function showInfo(d) {
  const panel = document.getElementById('info');
  panel.style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('i-name').textContent = d.label;
  document.getElementById('i-meta').textContent = `${PHASE_LABELS[d.phase]} · ${LAYER_LABELS[d.layer]} · ${d.type}`;
  const depDiv = document.getElementById('i-deps');
  depDiv.innerHTML = '';
  // outgoing
  const outgoing = links.filter(l => l.s === d.id);
  const incoming = links.filter(l => l.t === d.id);
  if (outgoing.length) {
    depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="section-title">Depends on (${outgoing.length})</div>`;
    outgoing.forEach(l => {
      const tgt = nodeMap[l.t];
      depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="dep"><span class="dir">→</span> ${tgt?.label||l.t} <span class="etype">[${EDGE_LABELS[l.type]}]${l.lbl?' '+l.lbl:''}</span></div>`;
    });
  }
  if (incoming.length) {
    depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="section-title">Used by (${incoming.length})</div>`;
    incoming.forEach(l => {
      const src = nodeMap[l.s];
      depDiv.innerHTML += `<div class="dep"><span class="dir">←</span> ${src?.label||l.s} <span class="etype">[${EDGE_LABELS[l.type]}]${l.lbl?' '+l.lbl:''}</span></div>`;
    });
  }
}

// Search
document.getElementById('search').addEventListener('input', e => {
  const q = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
  if (!q) { clearHL(); return; }
  const matches = nodes.filter(n => n.label.toLowerCase().includes(q) || n.id.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  if (!matches.length) { clearHL(); return; }
  const matchIds = new Set(matches.map(n => n.id));
  const connected = new Set(matchIds);
  links.forEach(l => {
    if (matchIds.has(l.s)) connected.add(l.t);
    if (matchIds.has(l.t)) connected.add(l.s);
  });
  nodeEls.classed('dimmed', n => !connected.has(n.id));
  nodeEls.classed('highlighted', n => matchIds.has(n.id));
  edgeEls.classed('dimmed', l => !(matchIds.has(l.s) || matchIds.has(l.t)));
  edgeEls.classed('highlighted', l => matchIds.has(l.s) || matchIds.has(l.t));
});

// Close info panel button
document.getElementById('info-close').onclick = () => clearHL();

// Initial fit — smaller scale on mobile
const initScale = window.innerWidth < 768 ? 0.45 : 0.7;
svg.call(zoom.transform, d3.zoomIdentity.translate(10, 0).scale(initScale));
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script type="importmap">
{
  "imports": {
    "three": "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.164.1/build/three.module.js",
    "three/addons/": "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/three@0.164.1/examples/jsm/"

<script type="module">
import * as THREE from 'three';
import { OrbitControls } from 'three/addons/controls/OrbitControls.js';

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DATA — identical to flat heatmap
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const PHASES=['all','a','a1','b','c','d'];
const PL={all:'All',a:'A',a1:'A1',b:'B',c:'C',d:'D'};
const PC={all:0xb89eff,a:0x6cb4ff,a1:0x7af0ff,b:0x45eaad,c:0xffd04a,d:0xff8080};
const LAYERS=['0-Core','1-Managers','2-Data','3-MonoBehaviours','4-Utils','5-Tests'];
const LL={'0-Core':'Core','1-Managers':'Mgrs','2-Data':'Data','3-MonoBehaviours':'Mono','4-Utils':'Utils','5-Tests':'Tests'};

const ET=['inherit','interface','get','set','event-sub','event-raise','singleton','creates','uses-util'];
const EC={inherit:0xb89eff,interface:0x7af0ff,get:0x5aeaad,set:0xff8080,'event-sub':0xffe066,'event-raise':0xffab57,singleton:0xd4a0ff,creates:0xff85c8,'uses-util':0x62bfff};
const EL={inherit:'Inherits',interface:'Interface',get:'Get()',set:'Set()','event-sub':'Event +=','event-raise':'Raise()','singleton':'Singleton.Ins','creates':'Creates','uses-util':'Utils call'};

const NM={
  GameEvents_All:{p:'all',l:'0-Core',n:'GameEvents(All)'},Singleton:{p:'all',l:'0-Core',n:'Singleton<T>'},
