// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BUILD AGGREGATED MATRIX
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const cellKeys = [];
PHASES.forEach(p => LAYERS.forEach(l => cellKeys.push(p+'|'+l)));
const activeCells = new Set();
ALL_EDGES.forEach(e => { const s=NM[e.s],t=NM[e.t]; if(s)activeCells.add(s.p+'|'+s.l); if(t)activeCells.add(t.p+'|'+t.l); });
const usedKeys = cellKeys.filter(k => activeCells.has(k));
const keyIndex = {}; usedKeys.forEach((k,i) => keyIndex[k]=i);

function cellLabel(k){ const[p,l]=k.split('|'); return PL[p]+'/'+LL[l]; }

let crossOnly = false;

function buildMatrix(){
  const mat = {};
  ALL_EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn=NM[e.s],tn=NM[e.t]; if(!sn||!tn) return;
    if(crossOnly && sn.p===tn.p) return;
    const sk=sn.p+'|'+sn.l, tk=tn.p+'|'+tn.l;
    const mk=sk+'>'+tk;
    if(!mat[mk]) mat[mk]={edges:[],byType:{}};
    mat[mk].edges.push(e);
    if(!mat[mk].byType[e.type]) mat[mk].byType[e.type]=[];
    mat[mk].byType[e.type].push(e);
  });
  return mat;
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// THREE.JS SCENE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const W=window.innerWidth, H=window.innerHeight;
const scene = new THREE.Scene();
scene.background = new THREE.Color(0x101014);
scene.fog = new THREE.FogExp2(0x101014, 0.012);

const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(50, W/H, 0.1, 200);
camera.position.set(20, 18, 28);

const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias:true });
renderer.setSize(W, H);
renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2));
renderer.shadowMap.enabled = true;
renderer.shadowMap.type = THREE.PCFSoftShadowMap;
renderer.toneMapping = THREE.ACESFilmicToneMapping;
renderer.toneMappingExposure = 1.2;
document.body.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

const controls = new OrbitControls(camera, renderer.domElement);
controls.enableDamping = true;
controls.dampingFactor = 0.08;
controls.target.set(usedKeys.length*0.5, 0, usedKeys.length*0.5);
controls.minDistance = 5;
controls.maxDistance = 80;
controls.maxPolarAngle = Math.PI * 0.48;
controls.update();

// Lights
const ambientLight = new THREE.AmbientLight(0x404060, 0.6);
scene.add(ambientLight);
const dirLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffeedd, 1.0);
dirLight.position.set(15, 25, 20);
dirLight.castShadow = true;
dirLight.shadow.mapSize.set(1024,1024);
dirLight.shadow.camera.near = 1; dirLight.shadow.camera.far = 60;
dirLight.shadow.camera.left=-30; dirLight.shadow.camera.right=30;
dirLight.shadow.camera.top=30; dirLight.shadow.camera.bottom=-30;
scene.add(dirLight);

const rimLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0x6688cc, 0.3);
rimLight.position.set(-10, 10, -15);
scene.add(rimLight);

// Ground plane
const N = usedKeys.length;
const groundGeo = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(N+4, N+4);
const groundMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color:0x12121a, roughness:0.95, metalness:0.1 });
const ground = new THREE.Mesh(groundGeo, groundMat);
ground.rotation.x = -Math.PI/2;
ground.position.set(N/2, -0.01, N/2);
ground.receiveShadow = true;
scene.add(ground);

// Grid lines on ground
const gridHelper = new THREE.GridHelper(N+2, N+2, 0x222233, 0x1a1a28);
gridHelper.position.set(N/2, 0, N/2);
scene.add(gridHelper);

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BUILD BARS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let bars = [];
const barGroup = new THREE.Group();
scene.add(barGroup);

// Axis label sprites
function makeLabel(text, position, color=0x808090, size=0.5) {
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  canvas.width = 512; canvas.height = 128;
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,512,128);
  ctx.font = 'bold 36px JetBrains Mono, monospace';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#'+color.toString(16).padStart(6,'0');
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
  ctx.fillText(text, 256, 64);
  const tex = new THREE.CanvasTexture(canvas);
  tex.minFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
  const mat = new THREE.SpriteMaterial({ map:tex, transparent:true, depthTest:false });
  const sprite = new THREE.Sprite(mat);
  sprite.position.copy(position);
  sprite.scale.set(size*5, size*1.25, 1);
  return sprite;
}
function makeBigLabel(text, position, color=0xe5a210, size=0.7) {
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  canvas.width = 1024; canvas.height = 128;
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,1024,128);
  ctx.font = 'bold 48px JetBrains Mono, monospace';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#'+color.toString(16).padStart(6,'0');
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
  ctx.fillText(text, 512, 64);
  const tex = new THREE.CanvasTexture(canvas);
  tex.minFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
  const mat = new THREE.SpriteMaterial({ map:tex, transparent:true, depthTest:false });
  const sprite = new THREE.Sprite(mat);
  sprite.position.copy(position);
  sprite.scale.set(size*8, size*1.5, 1);
  return sprite;
}

const labelGroup = new THREE.Group();
scene.add(labelGroup);

// Pre-compute phase and layer boundaries for region rendering
const phaseRanges = {}; // phase -> {start, end}
const layerRanges = {}; // layer -> {start, end}
usedKeys.forEach((k,i) => {
  const [p,l] = k.split('|');
  if (!phaseRanges[p]) phaseRanges[p] = {start:i, end:i};
  phaseRanges[p].end = i;
  if (!layerRanges[l]) layerRanges[l] = {start:i, end:i};
  layerRanges[l].end = i;
});

function buildBars() {
  // Clear old
  while(barGroup.children.length) barGroup.remove(barGroup.children[0]);
  while(labelGroup.children.length) labelGroup.remove(labelGroup.children[0]);
  bars = [];

  const matrix = buildMatrix();
  let maxCount = 1;
  Object.values(matrix).forEach(v => { if(v.edges.length > maxCount) maxCount = v.edges.length; });
  const heightScale = 8 / maxCount;

  // ── PHASE REGION STRIPS (colored ground strips along X and Z) ──
  Object.entries(phaseRanges).forEach(([p, range]) => {
    const len = range.end - range.start + 1;
    const mid = range.start + len/2;
    const color = PC[p];
    // X-axis strip (target columns)
    const stripGeoX = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(len, N+2);
    const stripMatX = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color, transparent:true, opacity:0.03, side:THREE.DoubleSide });
    const stripX = new THREE.Mesh(stripGeoX, stripMatX);
    stripX.rotation.x = -Math.PI/2;
    stripX.position.set(mid+0.5, 0.005, N/2);
    barGroup.add(stripX);
    // Z-axis strip (source rows)
    const stripGeoZ = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(N+2, len);
    const stripMatZ = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color, transparent:true, opacity:0.03, side:THREE.DoubleSide });
    const stripZ = new THREE.Mesh(stripGeoZ, stripMatZ);
    stripZ.rotation.x = -Math.PI/2;
    stripZ.position.set(N/2, 0.006, mid+0.5);
    barGroup.add(stripZ);
    // Phase boundary lines (vertical walls at boundaries)
    if (range.start > 0) {
      const lineGeo = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([
        new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0, -0.5),
        new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0.3, -0.5),
        new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0.3, N+0.5),
        new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0, N+0.5),
      ]);
      const lineMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color, transparent:true, opacity:0.4 });
      barGroup.add(new THREE.Line(lineGeo, lineMat));
      // Horizontal line on Z axis
      const lineGeoZ = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints([
        new THREE.Vector3(-0.5, 0, range.start),
        new THREE.Vector3(-0.5, 0.3, range.start),
        new THREE.Vector3(N+0.5, 0.3, range.start),
        new THREE.Vector3(N+0.5, 0, range.start),
      ]);
      barGroup.add(new THREE.Line(lineGeoZ, lineMat));
    }
    // Phase name label along X axis (big, at bottom)
    labelGroup.add(makeBigLabel('Phase-'+PL[p], new THREE.Vector3(mid+0.5, 0.5, N+3), color, 0.55));
    // Phase name label along Z axis
    labelGroup.add(makeBigLabel('Phase-'+PL[p], new THREE.Vector3(-3, 0.5, mid+0.5), color, 0.55));
  });

  // ── LAYER REGION LABELS (along both axes) ──
  Object.entries(layerRanges).forEach(([l, range]) => {
    const len = range.end - range.start + 1;
    const mid = range.start + len/2;
    // Layer label along X axis (below phase label)
    labelGroup.add(makeLabel(LL[l], new THREE.Vector3(mid+0.5, 0.15, N+1.8), 0x606080, 0.35));
    // Layer label along Z axis
    labelGroup.add(makeLabel(LL[l], new THREE.Vector3(-1.5, 0.15, mid+0.5), 0x606080, 0.35));
    // Subtle layer boundary lines
    if (range.start > 0) {
      const pts = [new THREE.Vector3(-0.3, 0.01, range.start), new THREE.Vector3(N+0.3, 0.01, range.start)];
      const lg = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints(pts);
      barGroup.add(new THREE.Line(lg, new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color:0x333344, transparent:true, opacity:0.3 })));
      const pts2 = [new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0.01, -0.3), new THREE.Vector3(range.start, 0.01, N+0.3)];
      const lg2 = new THREE.BufferGeometry().setFromPoints(pts2);
      barGroup.add(new THREE.Line(lg2, new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ color:0x333344, transparent:true, opacity:0.3 })));
    }
  });

  // ── CELL LABELS (per-cell) ──
  usedKeys.forEach((k,i) => {
    const [p] = k.split('|');
    labelGroup.add(makeLabel(cellLabel(k), new THREE.Vector3(-1.5, 0.6, i+0.5), PC[p], 0.3));
    labelGroup.add(makeLabel(cellLabel(k), new THREE.Vector3(i+0.5, 0.6, N+1.5), PC[p], 0.3));
  });
  // Axis titles
  labelGroup.add(makeBigLabel('SOURCE \u2192', new THREE.Vector3(-4.5, 1.0, N/2), 0xe5a210, 0.6));
  labelGroup.add(makeBigLabel('TARGET \u2192', new THREE.Vector3(N/2, 1.0, N+4.5), 0xe5a210, 0.6));

  // Base plates for each cell
  usedKeys.forEach((rk, ri) => {
    usedKeys.forEach((ck, ci) => {
      const mk = rk+'>'+ck;
      const data = matrix[mk];

      // Base tile
      const tileGeo = new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.9, 0.02, 0.9);
      const tileMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        color: rk===ck ? 0x1e1e2a : 0x16161e,
        roughness: 0.9, metalness: 0.0, transparent: true, opacity: 0.7
      });
      const tile = new THREE.Mesh(tileGeo, tileMat);
      tile.position.set(ci+0.5, 0, ri+0.5);
      tile.receiveShadow = true;
      barGroup.add(tile);

      if (!data || data.edges.length === 0) return;

      // Extruded bar
      const count = data.edges.length;
      const h = Math.max(0.15, count * heightScale);
      const dominant = Object.entries(data.byType).sort((a,b)=>b[1].length-a[1].length)[0][0];
      const color = EC[dominant];

      const barGeo = new THREE.BoxGeometry(0.7, h, 0.7);
      const barMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        color: color,
        roughness: 0.3,
        metalness: 0.5,
        emissive: color,
        emissiveIntensity: 0.15,
      });
      const bar = new THREE.Mesh(barGeo, barMat);
      bar.position.set(ci+0.5, h/2, ri+0.5);
      bar.castShadow = true;
      bar.receiveShadow = true;
      bar.userData = { srcKey:rk, tgtKey:ck, data, count, dominant };
      barGroup.add(bar);
      bars.push(bar);

      // Count label on top
      if (count >= 2) {
        const lbl = makeLabel(count.toString(), new THREE.Vector3(ci+0.5, h+0.25, ri+0.5), 0xffffff, 0.2);
        barGroup.add(lbl);
      }
    });
  });
}

buildBars();
buildStats();
buildLegend();

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RAYCASTING (hover + click)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const raycaster = new THREE.Raycaster();
const mouse = new THREE.Vector2();
let hoveredBar = null;
const tooltip = document.getElementById('tooltip');

renderer.domElement.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
  mouse.x = (e.clientX / window.innerWidth) * 2 - 1;
  mouse.y = -(e.clientY / window.innerHeight) * 2 + 1;
  raycaster.setFromCamera(mouse, camera);
  const hits = raycaster.intersectObjects(bars, false);

  if (hoveredBar) {
    hoveredBar.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.15;
    hoveredBar.scale.set(1,1,1);
  }

  if (hits.length > 0) {
    const bar = hits[0].object;
    if (bar.userData.data) {
      hoveredBar = bar;
      bar.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.5;
      bar.scale.set(1.08, 1.05, 1.08);
      const d = bar.userData;
      document.getElementById('tt-title').textContent = `${cellLabel(d.srcKey)} → ${cellLabel(d.tgtKey)}`;
      document.getElementById('tt-count').textContent = d.count + ' edge' + (d.count>1?'s':'');
      const types = Object.entries(d.data.byType).map(([t,e])=>`${EL[t]}: ${e.length}`).join(' · ');
      document.getElementById('tt-detail').textContent = types;
      tooltip.style.display = 'block';
      tooltip.style.left = (e.clientX + 16) + 'px';
      tooltip.style.top = (e.clientY - 10) + 'px';
      renderer.domElement.style.cursor = 'pointer';
    }
  } else {
    hoveredBar = null;
    tooltip.style.display = 'none';
    renderer.domElement.style.cursor = 'grab';
  }
});

renderer.domElement.addEventListener('click', e => {
  mouse.x = (e.clientX / window.innerWidth) * 2 - 1;
  mouse.y = -(e.clientY / window.innerHeight) * 2 + 1;
  raycaster.setFromCamera(mouse, camera);
  const hits = raycaster.intersectObjects(bars, false);
  if (hits.length > 0 && hits[0].object.userData.data) {
    showDetail(hits[0].object.userData);
  }
});

function showDetail(d) {
  const panel = document.getElementById('detail');
  panel.style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('det-title').textContent = `${cellLabel(d.srcKey)} → ${cellLabel(d.tgtKey)}`;
  document.getElementById('det-meta').textContent = `${d.count} dependency edges`;
  const el = document.getElementById('det-edges');
  el.innerHTML = '';
  Object.entries(d.data.byType).sort((a,b)=>b[1].length-a[1].length).forEach(([type, edges]) => {
    el.innerHTML += `<div class="d-section" style="color:#${EC[type].toString(16).padStart(6,'0')}">${EL[type]} (${edges.length})</div>`;
    edges.forEach(e => {
      el.innerHTML += `<div class="d-edge"><div class="d-dot" style="background:#${EC[e.type].toString(16).padStart(6,'0')}"></div><span>${NM[e.s]?.n||e.s}</span><span class="d-arrow">→</span><span>${NM[e.t]?.n||e.t}</span></div>`;
    });
  });
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// STATS + LEGEND
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildStats() {
  let total=0, cross=0, directCross=0, eventRouted=0;
  ALL_EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const s=NM[e.s],t=NM[e.t]; if(!s||!t) return;
    total++;
    if(s.p!==t.p){
      cross++;
      if(!['event-sub','event-raise','inherit','interface','uses-util'].includes(e.type)) directCross++;
      if(e.type==='event-sub'||e.type==='event-raise') eventRouted++;
    }
  });
  const crossPct = Math.round(cross/total*100);
  const directPct = Math.round(directCross/total*100);
  document.getElementById('stats').innerHTML = `
    <div class="stat-card"><h4>Total</h4><div class="val">${total}</div><div class="sub">edges</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><h4>Intra-Phase</h4><div class="val">${total-cross}</div><div class="sub">${100-crossPct}%</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card ${crossPct>60?'bad':crossPct>40?'warn':'good'}"><h4>Cross-Phase</h4><div class="val">${cross}</div><div class="sub">${crossPct}%</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card ${directPct>20?'bad':directPct>10?'warn':'good'}"><h4>Direct X-Phase</h4><div class="val">${directCross}</div><div class="sub">${directPct}% coupling smell</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card good"><h4>Event-Routed</h4><div class="val">${eventRouted}</div><div class="sub">decoupled</div></div>
  `;
}

function buildLegend() {
  const el = document.getElementById('legend');
  ET.forEach(t => {
    el.innerHTML += `<div class="leg-row"><div class="leg-sq" style="background:#${EC[t].toString(16).padStart(6,'0')}"></div>${EL[t]}</div>`;
  });
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MODE TOGGLES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
document.getElementById('btn-all').onclick = () => {
  crossOnly=false;
  document.getElementById('btn-all').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('btn-cross').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('detail').style.display='none';
  buildBars(); buildStats();
};
document.getElementById('btn-cross').onclick = () => {
  crossOnly=true;
  document.getElementById('btn-cross').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('btn-all').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('detail').style.display='none';
  buildBars(); buildStats();
};
document.getElementById('btn-reset').onclick = () => {
  camera.position.set(20, 18, 28);
  controls.target.set(N*0.5, 0, N*0.5);
  controls.update();
};

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ANIMATION LOOP
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function animate() {
  requestAnimationFrame(animate);
  controls.update();
  renderer.render(scene, camera);
}
animate();

// Resize
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
  const w=window.innerWidth, h=window.innerHeight;
  camera.aspect = w/h;
  camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
  renderer.setSize(w,h);
});
</script>

<script>
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BUILD CELL KEYS: "phase|layer"
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const cellKeys = [];
PHASES.forEach(p => LAYERS.forEach(l => cellKeys.push(p+'|'+l)));

function cellLabel(key) {
  const [p,l] = key.split('|');
  return PHASE_LABELS[p] + '/' + LAYER_SHORT[l];
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AGGREGATE EDGES INTO CELL PAIRS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let crossOnly = false;

function buildMatrix() {
  const matrix = {}; // "srcKey|tgtKey" → { edges:[], byType:{} }
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (!sn || !tn) return;
    const sk = sn.p + '|' + sn.l;
    const tk = tn.p + '|' + tn.l;
    if (crossOnly && sn.p === tn.p) return; // skip intra-phase
    const mk = sk + '>' + tk;
    if (!matrix[mk]) matrix[mk] = { edges: [], byType: {} };
    matrix[mk].edges.push(e);
    if (!matrix[mk].byType[e.type]) matrix[mk].byType[e.type] = [];
    matrix[mk].byType[e.type].push(e);
  });
  return matrix;
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RENDER MATRIX
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function render() {
  const matrix = buildMatrix();
  const container = document.getElementById('matrix-container');
  container.innerHTML = '';

  // Determine which cellKeys have any data
  const activeCells = new Set();
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (sn) activeCells.add(sn.p + '|' + sn.l);
    if (tn) activeCells.add(tn.p + '|' + tn.l);
  });
  const usedKeys = cellKeys.filter(k => activeCells.has(k));

  const table = document.createElement('table');
  table.className = 'matrix';

  // Header row
  const thead = table.createTHead();
  const hrow = thead.insertRow();
  hrow.insertCell().textContent = ''; // corner
  let prevPhase = '';
  usedKeys.forEach(k => {
    const th = document.createElement('th');
    th.className = 'col-header';
    const [p] = k.split('|');
    if (p !== prevPhase && prevPhase) th.classList.add('phase-sep');
    prevPhase = p;
    th.textContent = cellLabel(k);
    th.style.color = PHASE_COLORS[p];
    hrow.appendChild(th);
  });

  // Data rows — with phase group headers
  const tbody = table.createTBody();
  let prevRowPhase = '';
  usedKeys.forEach((rk, ri) => {
    const [rp, rl] = rk.split('|');
    // Insert phase group header row when phase changes
    if (rp !== prevRowPhase) {
      const gtr = tbody.insertRow();
      const gth = document.createElement('th');
      gth.className = 'row-header';
      gth.style.color = PHASE_COLORS[rp];
      gth.style.fontSize = '10px';
      gth.style.fontWeight = '700';
      gth.style.paddingTop = ri > 0 ? '8px' : '2px';
      gth.textContent = 'Phase-' + PHASE_LABELS[rp];
      gtr.appendChild(gth);
      // fill remaining cells as empty spacers
      usedKeys.forEach(() => {
        const spacer = gtr.insertCell();
        spacer.className = 'phase-group-cell';
      });
    }
    prevRowPhase = rp;
    const tr = tbody.insertRow();
    const rth = document.createElement('th');
    rth.className = 'row-header';
    rth.textContent = cellLabel(rk);
    rth.style.color = PHASE_COLORS[rp];
    tr.appendChild(rth);

    let prevColPhase = '';
    usedKeys.forEach((ck, ci) => {
      const td = tr.insertCell();
      const [cp] = ck.split('|');
      if (cp !== prevColPhase && prevColPhase) td.classList.add('phase-sep');
      prevColPhase = cp;
      if (rk === ck) td.classList.add('diagonal');

      const mk = rk + '>' + ck;
      const data = matrix[mk];
      if (!data || data.edges.length === 0) {
        td.classList.add('empty');
        return;
      }
      const count = data.edges.length;
      // Color: blend dominant edge type
      const dominantType = Object.entries(data.byType).sort((a,b) => b[1].length - a[1].length)[0][0];
      const baseColor = EDGE_COLORS[dominantType];
      const intensity = Math.min(1, count / 8);
      td.style.background = hexWithAlpha(baseColor, 0.15 + intensity * 0.75);
      td.innerHTML = `<span class="cell-count">${count}</span>`;

      // Is this cross-phase?
      const isCross = rp !== cp;
      if (isCross) td.style.outline = '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)';

      td.title = `${cellLabel(rk)} → ${cellLabel(ck)}: ${count} edges`;
      td.onclick = () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('td.selected').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('selected'));
        td.classList.add('selected');
        showDetail(rk, ck, data);
      };
    });
  });

  container.appendChild(table);

  // Stats
  renderSummary(matrix, usedKeys);
  renderVerdict(matrix);
  renderLegend();
}

function hexWithAlpha(hex, alpha) {
  const r = parseInt(hex.slice(1,3),16), g = parseInt(hex.slice(3,5),16), b = parseInt(hex.slice(5,7),16);
  return `rgba(${r},${g},${b},${alpha})`;
}

function renderLegend() {
  const el = document.getElementById('matrix-legend');
  let html = '';
  EDGE_TYPES.forEach(t => {
    html += `<div class="ml-item"><div class="ml-swatch" style="background:${EDGE_COLORS[t]}"></div>${EDGE_LABELS[t]}</div>`;
  });
  html += `<div class="ml-item" style="color:var(--muted);margin-left:8px;">brightness = edge count</div>`;
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderSummary(matrix, usedKeys) {
  const el = document.getElementById('summary');
  const totalEdges = EDGES.filter(e => NM[e.s] && NM[e.t]).length;
  let crossPhaseEdges = 0, intraPhaseEdges = 0;
  let crossPhaseDirectEdges = 0; // non-event, non-inherit, non-interface cross-phase
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (!sn || !tn) return;
    if (sn.p !== tn.p) {
      crossPhaseEdges++;
      if (!['event-sub','event-raise','inherit','interface','uses-util'].includes(e.type)) crossPhaseDirectEdges++;
    } else intraPhaseEdges++;
  });
  const crossPct = Math.round(crossPhaseEdges / totalEdges * 100);
  const directCrossPct = Math.round(crossPhaseDirectEdges / totalEdges * 100);

  // Count event-routed cross-phase
  let eventRouted = 0;
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (!sn || !tn) return;
    if (sn.p !== tn.p && (e.type === 'event-sub' || e.type === 'event-raise')) eventRouted++;
  });

  el.innerHTML = `
    <div class="summary-card"><h4>Total Edges</h4><div class="val">${totalEdges}</div><div class="sub">across all phases</div></div>
    <div class="summary-card"><h4>Intra-Phase</h4><div class="val">${intraPhaseEdges}</div><div class="sub">${100-crossPct}% — same-phase deps</div></div>
    <div class="summary-card ${crossPct > 60 ? 'bad' : crossPct > 40 ? 'warn' : 'good'}"><h4>Cross-Phase</h4><div class="val">${crossPhaseEdges}</div><div class="sub">${crossPct}% — cross-phase deps</div></div>
    <div class="summary-card ${directCrossPct > 20 ? 'bad' : directCrossPct > 10 ? 'warn' : 'good'}"><h4>Direct Cross-Phase</h4><div class="val">${crossPhaseDirectEdges}</div><div class="sub">${directCrossPct}% — Get/Set/Singleton across phases (coupling smell)</div></div>
    <div class="summary-card good"><h4>Event-Routed</h4><div class="val">${eventRouted}</div><div class="sub">cross-phase via GameEvents (decoupled)</div></div>
  `;
}

function renderVerdict(matrix) {
  const el = document.getElementById('verdict');
  // Analyze: find the worst cross-phase direct couplings
  const crossDirect = {};
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (!sn || !tn || sn.p === tn.p) return;
    if (['event-sub','event-raise','inherit','interface','uses-util'].includes(e.type)) return;
    const key = `${sn.p}→${tn.p}`;
    if (!crossDirect[key]) crossDirect[key] = [];
    crossDirect[key].push(e);
  });

  let verdictHTML = '<h3>COUPLING VERDICT</h3>';

  // Good patterns
  verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row"><span class="v-icon v-good">✓</span><div class="v-text">All cross-phase communication is routed through <b>GameEvents</b> (event bus pattern). No direct Mono→Mono calls across phases.</div></div>`;
  verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row"><span class="v-icon v-good">✓</span><div class="v-text"><b>Inheritance</b> is correctly downward: tools→BaseHeldTool→BaseSellable→BasePhysObj. No circular inheritance.</div></div>`;
  verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row"><span class="v-icon v-good">✓</span><div class="v-text"><b>Interfaces</b> (IInteractable, IDamageable, IIconItem) are in Data layers — implemented by Mono layers. Correct dependency direction.</div></div>`;

  // Cross-phase singleton reads (acceptable but notable)
  const singletonCross = [];
  EDGES.forEach(e => {
    const sn = NM[e.s], tn = NM[e.t];
    if (!sn || !tn || sn.p === tn.p || e.type !== 'singleton') return;
    singletonCross.push(e);
  });
  if (singletonCross.length > 0) {
    verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row"><span class="v-icon v-warn">⚠</span><div class="v-text"><b>${singletonCross.length} cross-phase Singleton reads</b> — acceptable for legitimate queries (EconomyManager.GetMoney, UIManager.isAnyMenuOpen, OreLimitManager.ShouldBlock). These are read-only and don't create write-coupling.</div></div>`;
  }

  // Direct cross-phase Get/Set/Creates
  Object.entries(crossDirect).forEach(([key, edges]) => {
    const types = [...new Set(edges.map(e => e.type))].join(', ');
    const names = edges.slice(0, 3).map(e => `${NM[e.s].n}→${NM[e.t].n}`).join(', ');
    const more = edges.length > 3 ? ` +${edges.length-3} more` : '';
    if (edges.some(e => e.type === 'singleton')) return; // already covered above
    verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row"><span class="v-icon v-warn">⚠</span><div class="v-text"><b>${key}</b>: ${edges.length} direct deps [${types}] — ${names}${more}</div></div>`;
  });

  verdictHTML += `<div class="v-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><span class="v-icon v-good">★</span><div class="v-text" style="color:var(--accent);font-weight:600;">Overall: <b>Well-decoupled architecture.</b> Cross-phase deps are either event-routed, inheritance chains, or read-only singleton queries. No write-coupling across phase boundaries.</div></div>`;

  el.innerHTML = verdictHTML;
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DETAIL PANEL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function showDetail(srcKey, tgtKey, data) {
  const panel = document.getElementById('detail-panel');
  panel.style.display = 'block';
  const [sp] = srcKey.split('|'), [tp] = tgtKey.split('|');
  const isCross = sp !== tp;
  document.getElementById('d-title').textContent = `${cellLabel(srcKey)} → ${cellLabel(tgtKey)}`;
  const crossBadge = isCross ? ' · <span style="color:#ff8080">cross-phase</span>' : ' · <span style="color:#45eaad">intra-phase</span>';
  document.getElementById('d-meta').innerHTML = `${data.edges.length} dependency edge${data.edges.length>1?'s':''}${crossBadge}`;

  // Mini summary: counts per type
  const sumArea = document.getElementById('d-summary-area');
  const sorted = Object.entries(data.byType).sort((a,b) => b[1].length - a[1].length);
  let sumHTML = '<div class="d-summary">';
  sorted.forEach(([type, edges]) => {
    sumHTML += `<div class="d-stat"><div class="d-stat-label">${EDGE_LABELS[type]}</div><div class="d-stat-val" style="color:${EDGE_COLORS[type]}">${edges.length}</div></div>`;
  });
  sumHTML += '</div>';
  sumArea.innerHTML = sumHTML;

  // Type distribution bar
  const barEl = document.getElementById('d-type-bar');
  let barHTML = '';
  sorted.forEach(([type, edges]) => {
    const pct = (edges.length / data.edges.length * 100);
    barHTML += `<div class="d-type-seg" style="width:${pct}%;background:${EDGE_COLORS[type]}" title="${EDGE_LABELS[type]}: ${edges.length}"></div>`;
  });
  barEl.innerHTML = barHTML;

  // Edge list grouped by type
  const el = document.getElementById('d-edges');
  el.innerHTML = '';
  sorted.forEach(([type, edges]) => {
    el.innerHTML += `<div style="margin-top:8px;font-size:9px;color:${EDGE_COLORS[type]};font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;">${EDGE_LABELS[type]} (${edges.length})</div>`;
    edges.forEach(e => {
      el.innerHTML += `<div class="edge-item">
        <div class="edge-dot" style="background:${EDGE_COLORS[e.type]}"></div>
        <span class="edge-from">${NM[e.s]?.n||e.s}</span>
        <span class="edge-arrow">→</span>
        <span class="edge-to">${NM[e.t]?.n||e.t}</span>
        ${e.lbl ? `<span class="edge-label">${e.lbl}</span>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    });
  });
}

// Close detail panel
document.getElementById('detail-close').onclick = () => {
  document.getElementById('detail-panel').style.display = 'none';
  document.querySelectorAll('td.selected').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('selected'));
};

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MODE TOGGLE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
document.getElementById('btn-all').onclick = () => {
  crossOnly = false;
  document.getElementById('btn-all').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('btn-cross').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('detail-panel').style.display = 'none';
  render();
};
document.getElementById('btn-cross').onclick = () => {
  crossOnly = true;
  document.getElementById('btn-cross').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('btn-all').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('detail-panel').style.display = 'none';
  render();
};

// Initial render
render();
</script>
</body>

<!-- ==== FILE: web-tools/pack.js ==== -->
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const DELIMITER_PREFIX = '<!-- ==== FILE: ';
const DELIMITER_SUFFIX = ' ==== -->';

function getAllFiles(dirPath) {
    let results = [];
    for (const entry of fs.readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true })) {
        const fullPath = path.join(dirPath, entry.name);
        if (entry.isDirectory()) results = results.concat(getAllFiles(fullPath));
        else results.push(fullPath);
    }
    return results.sort();
}

const targetDir = process.argv[2];
if (!targetDir) { console.error('Usage: node pack.js <folder>'); process.exit(1); }
if (!fs.existsSync(targetDir)) { console.error(`Folder not found: ${targetDir}`); process.exit(1); }

const folderName = path.basename(targetDir);
const outputFile = folderName + '.txt';
const files = getAllFiles(targetDir);
let packed = '';

for (const filePath of files) {
    const relativePath = folderName + '/' + path.relative(targetDir, filePath).replace(/\\/g, '/');
    const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
    packed += DELIMITER_PREFIX + relativePath + DELIMITER_SUFFIX + '\n' + content;
    if (!content.endsWith('\n')) packed += '\n';
    packed += '\n';
}

fs.writeFileSync(outputFile, packed, 'utf8');
console.log(`Packed ${files.length} files -> ${outputFile}`);
// used in terminal(powershell) after in the dir of pack.js as following command:
// node pack.js "learn/phase-b(New)"

<script>
// ── Constants ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
const DELIMITER_RE = /^<!-- ==== FILE: (.+) ==== -->$/;
const LINE_LIMIT   = 100000;
const LINKS_KEY    = 'phase_viewer_links';

// ── State ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let state = {
    files: {},
    rootName: '',
    selectedPath: null,
    mdRendered: true,
    htmlRendered: false,
    fullContent: {},
    sidebarOpen: false,
    sidebarCollapsed: false,
    isFullscreen: false,
};

// ── Element refs ───────────────────────────────────────────────
const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);
const landing        = $('landing');
const viewer         = $('viewer');
const treeContainer  = $('tree-container');
const codeWrapper    = $('code-wrapper');
const breadcrumb     = $('breadcrumb');
const contentToolbar = $('content-toolbar');
const sidebar        = $('sidebar');
const resizer        = $('resizer');

// ── URL History Storage ────────────────────────────────────────
function loadLinks() {
    try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LINKS_KEY) || '[]'); }
    catch { return []; }
}

function saveLink(url) {
    const links = loadLinks();
    const already = links.some(l => l.url === url);
    if (already) return;
    links.unshift({ url, ts: Date.now() });
    // keep at most 40
    if (links.length > 40) links.splice(40);
    localStorage.setItem(LINKS_KEY, JSON.stringify(links));
    renderUrlHistory();
}

function deleteLink(url) {
    const links = loadLinks().filter(l => l.url !== url);
    localStorage.setItem(LINKS_KEY, JSON.stringify(links));
    renderUrlHistory();
}

function formatRelTime(ts) {
    const sec = Math.floor((Date.now() - ts) / 1000);
    if (sec < 60) return 'just now';
    if (sec < 3600) return Math.floor(sec / 60) + 'm ago';
    if (sec < 86400) return Math.floor(sec / 3600) + 'h ago';
    return Math.floor(sec / 86400) + 'd ago';
}

function esc(s) {
    return s.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
}

function renderUrlHistory() {
    const list  = $('url-history-list');
    const empty = $('url-history-empty');
    const links = loadLinks();

    Array.from(list.querySelectorAll('.url-card')).forEach(c => c.remove());

    if (links.length === 0) {
        empty.style.display = '';
        return;
    }
    empty.style.display = 'none';

    for (const item of links) {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'url-card';
        const label = item.url.split('/').pop() || item.url;
        const shortUrl = item.url.length > 55 ? item.url.slice(0, 55) + '…' : item.url;
        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="url-card-badge">📦</div>
            <div class="url-card-body">
                <div class="url-card-name" title="${esc(label)}">${esc(label)}</div>
                <div class="url-card-meta">
                    <span class="url-card-meta-url" title="${esc(item.url)}">${esc(shortUrl)}</span>
                    <span class="url-card-meta-ts">${esc(formatRelTime(item.ts))}</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <button class="url-card-del" title="Remove">✕</button>
        `;
        card.querySelector('.url-card-del').addEventListener('click', e => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            deleteLink(item.url);
        });
        card.addEventListener('click', () => {
            $('landing-url').value = item.url;
            fetchUrl(item.url);
        });
        list.appendChild(card);
    }
}

$('url-history-clear').addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (!confirm('Clear all saved links? This cannot be undone.')) return;
    localStorage.removeItem(LINKS_KEY);
    renderUrlHistory();
});

// Render on load
renderUrlHistory();

// ── Logo → Home ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function goHome() {
    // If viewer is active, go back to landing
    if (viewer.classList.contains('active')) {
        viewer.classList.remove('active');
        landing.style.display = '';
        $('btn-download-zip').style.display = 'none';
        $('btn-reset').style.display = 'none';
        // Keep state so user can come back
    } else {
        // Already on landing, just scroll to top
        landing.scrollTop = 0;
    }
    exitFullscreen();
}

$('logo').addEventListener('click', goHome);
$('logo').addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') goHome(); });

// ── Parser ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function parsePacked(text) {
    const files = {};
    const lines = text.split('\n');
    let currentPath = null;
    let currentLines = [];

    function flush() {
        if (currentPath === null) return;
        let content = currentLines.join('\n');
        if (content.endsWith('\n')) content = content.slice(0, -1);
        files[currentPath] = content;
    }

    for (const line of lines) {
        const m = line.match(DELIMITER_RE);
        if (m) {
            flush();
            currentPath = m[1].trim();
            currentLines = [];
        } else if (currentPath !== null) {
            currentLines.push(line);
        }
    }
    flush();
    return files;
}

// ── Language detection ─────────────────────────────────────────
function detectLang(path) {
    const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    const map = {
        cs: 'csharp', md: 'markdown', json: 'json',
        xml: 'xml', html: 'html', js: 'javascript',
        ts: 'typescript', py: 'python', txt: 'plaintext',
        yaml: 'yaml', yml: 'yaml', sh: 'bash', bash: 'bash',
        go: 'go', rs: 'rust', java: 'java', cpp: 'cpp', cc: 'cpp',
        c: 'c', h: 'c', css: 'css', sql: 'sql',
        kt: 'kotlin', swift: 'swift', rb: 'ruby', php: 'php',
        ps1: 'powershell', dockerfile: 'dockerfile', toml: 'toml',
    };
    return map[ext] || 'plaintext';
}

function fileIcon(name) {
    const ext = name.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    const icons = {
        md: '📝', json: '📋', html: '🌐', xml: '📄', css: '🎨',
        js: '⚡', ts: '⚡', py: '🐍', rs: '🦀', go: '🐹',
        sh: '⚙', bash: '⚙', sql: '🗃', yaml: '⚙', yml: '⚙',
        cs: '🔷', java: '☕', kt: '🔶', swift: '🍎', rb: '💎',
        dockerfile: '🐳',
    };
    return icons[ext] || '📄';
}

// ── Marked renderer (advanced) ─────────────────────────────────
function buildMarkedRenderer() {
    const renderer = new marked.Renderer();

    // Code blocks with header (language badge + copy button)
    renderer.code = function(code, lang) {
        const safeLang = (lang || '').toLowerCase().trim().split(/\s/)[0];
        const validLang = safeLang && hljs.getLanguage(safeLang) ? safeLang : null;
        let highlighted;
        if (validLang) {
            try { highlighted = hljs.highlight(code, { language: validLang }).value; }
            catch { highlighted = hljs.highlightAuto(code).value; }
        } else {
            highlighted = hljs.highlightAuto(code).value;
        }
        const langDisplay = safeLang || 'text';
        // Escape raw code for data attribute
        const escapedCode = code.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#39;');
        return `<div class="code-block-wrap"><div class="code-hdr"><span class="lang-badge">${esc(langDisplay)}</span><button class="ccopy" onclick="copyCodeBlock(this)" data-code="${escapedCode}">⎘ Copy</button></div><pre><code class="hljs">${highlighted}</code></pre></div>`;
    };

    // Tables with scrollable wrapper
    renderer.table = function(header, body) {
        return `<div class="tbl-wrap"><table><thead>${header}</thead><tbody>${body}</tbody></table></div>`;
    };

    return renderer;
}

window.copyCodeBlock = function(btn) {
    const code = btn.getAttribute('data-code')
        .replace(/&amp;/g,'&').replace(/&lt;/g,'<').replace(/&gt;/g,'>').replace(/&quot;/g,'"').replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(() => {
        btn.textContent = '✓ Copied';
        btn.classList.add('ok');
        setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = '⎘ Copy'; btn.classList.remove('ok'); }, 1800);
    }).catch(() => {
        const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
        ta.value = code; document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy'); ta.remove();
        btn.textContent = '✓ Copied'; btn.classList.add('ok');
        setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = '⎘ Copy'; btn.classList.remove('ok'); }, 1800);
    });
};

// ── Tree building ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function buildTree(files) {
    const root = {};
    for (const path of Object.keys(files)) {
        const parts = path.split('/');
        let node = root;
        for (let i = 0; i < parts.length - 1; i++) {
            const p = parts[i];
            if (!node[p]) node[p] = { __type: 'dir', __children: {} };
            node = node[p].__children;
        }
        const fname = parts[parts.length - 1];
        node[fname] = { __type: 'file', __path: path };
    }
    return root;
}

function renderTreeNode(obj, depth, container) {
    const entries = Object.entries(obj).filter(([k]) => !k.startsWith('__'));
    const dirs  = entries.filter(([,v]) => v.__type === 'dir').sort(([a],[b]) => a.localeCompare(b));
    const files = entries.filter(([,v]) => v.__type === 'file').sort(([a],[b]) => a.localeCompare(b));

    for (const [name, node] of [...dirs, ...files]) {
        const isDir = node.__type === 'dir';
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        wrapper.className = 'tree-node';

        const item = document.createElement('div');
        item.className = 'tree-item';
        item.style.setProperty('--depth', depth);

        if (isDir) {
            const arrow = document.createElement('span');
            arrow.className = 'tree-arrow open';
            arrow.textContent = '▶';

            const icon = document.createElement('span');
            icon.className = 'tree-icon';
            icon.textContent = '📂';

            const label = document.createElement('span');
            label.className = 'tree-label';
            label.textContent = name;

            item.append(arrow, icon, label);

            const children = document.createElement('div');
            children.className = 'tree-children open';
            renderTreeNode(node.__children, depth + 1, children);

            item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const open = children.classList.toggle('open');
                arrow.classList.toggle('open', open);
                icon.textContent = open ? '📂' : '📁';
                if (e.altKey) {
                    children.querySelectorAll('.tree-children').forEach(c => c.classList.toggle('open', open));
                    children.querySelectorAll('.tree-arrow').forEach(a => a.classList.toggle('open', open));
                    children.querySelectorAll('.tree-item .tree-icon').forEach(ic => {
                        if (ic.textContent === '📂' || ic.textContent === '📁') ic.textContent = open ? '📂' : '📁';
                    });
                }
            });

            wrapper.append(item, children);
        } else {
            const spacer = document.createElement('span');
            spacer.style.width = '12px';
            spacer.style.display = 'inline-block';

            const icon = document.createElement('span');
            icon.className = 'tree-icon';
            icon.textContent = fileIcon(name);

            const label = document.createElement('span');
            label.className = 'tree-label';
            label.textContent = name;

            item.dataset.path = node.__path;
            item.append(spacer, icon, label);
            item.addEventListener('click', () => selectFile(node.__path));

            wrapper.append(item);
        }

        container.appendChild(wrapper);
    }
}

// ── File selection ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function selectFile(path) {
    state.selectedPath = path;
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-item.selected').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('selected'));
    const el = document.querySelector(`.tree-item[data-path="${CSS.escape(path)}"]`);
    if (el) {
        el.classList.add('selected');
        el.scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
    }
    if (window.innerWidth <= 680) {
        sidebar.classList.remove('open');
        state.sidebarOpen = false;
    }
    renderFile(path);
}

function renderFile(path) {
    const content = state.files[path] ?? '';
    const lang = detectLang(path);
    const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();

    // Breadcrumb
    const parts = path.split('/');
    breadcrumb.innerHTML = parts.map((p, i) => {
        const cls = i === parts.length - 1 ? 'bc-part last' : 'bc-part';
        return `<span class="${cls}">${p}</span>${i < parts.length - 1 ? '<span class="bc-sep">/</span>' : ''}`;
    }).join('');

    contentToolbar.style.display = 'flex';
    $('toolbar-lang').textContent = lang;

    const isMd = ext === 'md';
    const isHtml = ext === 'html' || ext === 'htm';
    const mdToggle = $('btn-md-toggle');
    const htmlToggle = $('btn-html-toggle');
    mdToggle.style.display = isMd ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
    htmlToggle.style.display = isHtml ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
    state.mdRendered = true;
    state.htmlRendered = false;
    if (isMd) mdToggle.textContent = '📝 Raw';
    if (isHtml) htmlToggle.textContent = '👁 Preview';

    const lines = content.split('\n');
    $('st-viewing').textContent = parts[parts.length - 1];
    $('st-lang').textContent = lang;
    $('st-lines').textContent = lines.length.toLocaleString();

    const truncNotice = $('truncation-notice');
    const needsTrunc = lines.length > LINE_LIMIT;
    state.fullContent[path] = content;

    if (needsTrunc) {
        truncNotice.style.display = 'flex';
        $('truncation-text').textContent =
            `⚠ File has ${lines.length.toLocaleString()} lines — showing first ${LINE_LIMIT.toLocaleString()}.`;
    } else {
        truncNotice.style.display = 'none';
    }

    const displayContent = needsTrunc ? lines.slice(0, LINE_LIMIT).join('\n') : content;
    _renderContent(displayContent, lang, ext, isMd);
}

function _renderContent(content, lang, ext, isMd) {
    codeWrapper.innerHTML = '';

    // HTML live preview (use full content for intact document)
    if ((ext === 'html' || ext === 'htm') && state.htmlRendered) {
        const iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
        iframe.id = 'html-preview-frame';
        iframe.sandbox = 'allow-scripts';
        iframe.srcdoc = state.files[state.selectedPath] || content;
        codeWrapper.appendChild(iframe);
        return;
    }

    if (isMd && state.mdRendered) {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.id = 'md-rendered';
        marked.setOptions({
            gfm: true,
            breaks: false,
            renderer: buildMarkedRenderer()
        });
        div.innerHTML = marked.parse(content);
        // Apply hljs to any code blocks that weren't handled by renderer (fallback)
        div.querySelectorAll('pre code:not(.hljs)').forEach(block => {
            hljs.highlightElement(block);
        });
        codeWrapper.appendChild(div);
        return;
    }

    const displayContent = content.replace(/\t/g, '    ');
    const lines = displayContent.split('\n');

    const lineNumsEl = document.createElement('div');
    lineNumsEl.id = 'line-numbers';
    const pad = lines.length.toString().length;
    lineNumsEl.textContent = lines.map((_, i) =>
        String(i + 1).padStart(pad)
    ).join('\n');

    const codeBody = document.createElement('div');
    codeBody.id = 'code-body';

    const codeEl = document.createElement('code');

    let hlLang = lang;
    if (hlLang === 'plaintext') hlLang = null;

    if (hlLang && hljs.getLanguage(hlLang)) {
        codeEl.className = `language-${hlLang}`;
        codeEl.textContent = displayContent;
        hljs.highlightElement(codeEl);
    } else {
        codeEl.textContent = displayContent;
        codeEl.style.color = 'var(--text-primary)';
    }

    codeBody.appendChild(codeEl);

    const wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.id = 'code-view-wrap';
    wrap.append(lineNumsEl, codeBody);
    codeWrapper.appendChild(wrap);
}

// ── Preview Width & Font Size Controls ─────────────────────────
const previewWidthSlider = $('preview-width-slider');
const previewWidthVal    = $('preview-width-val');
const fontSizeSlider     = $('font-size-slider');
const fontSizeVal        = $('font-size-val');

// Restore saved values
const savedPW = localStorage.getItem('phase_preview_width');
const savedFS = localStorage.getItem('phase_font_size');
if (savedPW) { previewWidthSlider.value = savedPW; }
if (savedFS) { fontSizeSlider.value     = savedFS; }

function applyPreviewWidth(val) {
    // val is a number string like "95" → set as 95% of the #code-wrapper
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--preview-width', val + '%');
    previewWidthVal.textContent = val + '%';
}
function applyFontSize(val) {
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--md-font-size', val + 'px');
    fontSizeVal.textContent = val + 'px';
}

applyPreviewWidth(previewWidthSlider.value);
applyFontSize(fontSizeSlider.value);

previewWidthSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
    applyPreviewWidth(previewWidthSlider.value);
    localStorage.setItem('phase_preview_width', previewWidthSlider.value);
});
fontSizeSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
    applyFontSize(fontSizeSlider.value);
    localStorage.setItem('phase_font_size', fontSizeSlider.value);
});

// ── Sidebar hide / show ────────────────────────────────────────
const btnToggleSidebar  = $('btn-toggle-sidebar');
const btnSidebarReveal  = $('btn-sidebar-reveal');

function setSidebarCollapsed(collapsed, skipSave) {
    state.sidebarCollapsed = collapsed;
    sidebar.classList.toggle('collapsed', collapsed);
    resizer.classList.toggle('collapsed', collapsed);
    btnToggleSidebar.textContent = collapsed ? '▶' : '◀';
    btnToggleSidebar.title = collapsed ? 'Show sidebar' : 'Hide sidebar';
    btnSidebarReveal.style.display = collapsed ? 'flex' : 'none';
    if (!skipSave) localStorage.setItem('phase_sidebar_collapsed', collapsed ? '1' : '0');
}

// Restore sidebar collapsed state
if (localStorage.getItem('phase_sidebar_collapsed') === '1') {
    setSidebarCollapsed(true, true);
}

// Restore sidebar width
const savedSidebarW = localStorage.getItem('phase_sidebar_width');
if (savedSidebarW) {
    const w = parseInt(savedSidebarW, 10);
    if (w >= 160 && w <= 500) {
        sidebar.style.width    = w + 'px';
        sidebar.style.minWidth = w + 'px';
        sidebar.style.maxWidth = w + 'px';
    }
}

btnToggleSidebar.addEventListener('click', () => setSidebarCollapsed(!state.sidebarCollapsed));
btnSidebarReveal.addEventListener('click', () => setSidebarCollapsed(false));

// ── Fullscreen (native browser API) ────────────────────────────
function enterFullscreen() {
    if (state.isFullscreen) return;
    const el = document.documentElement;
    const rfs = el.requestFullscreen || el.webkitRequestFullscreen || el.msRequestFullscreen;
    if (rfs) rfs.call(el);
    state.isFullscreen = true;
    document.body.classList.add('fullscreen-mode');
}

function exitFullscreen() {
    if (!state.isFullscreen) return;
    const efs = document.exitFullscreen || document.webkitExitFullscreen || document.msExitFullscreen;
    if (efs && document.fullscreenElement) efs.call(document);
    state.isFullscreen = false;
    document.body.classList.remove('fullscreen-mode');
}

// Sync state when browser exits fullscreen natively (e.g. Esc key)
document.addEventListener('fullscreenchange', () => {
    if (!document.fullscreenElement && state.isFullscreen) {
        state.isFullscreen = false;
        document.body.classList.remove('fullscreen-mode');
    }
});

$('btn-fullscreen').addEventListener('click', enterFullscreen);
$('fullscreen-exit-btn').addEventListener('click', exitFullscreen);

document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if (e.key === 'F11' && viewer.classList.contains('active')) {
        e.preventDefault();
        state.isFullscreen ? exitFullscreen() : enterFullscreen();
    }
});

// ── MD toggle ─────────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-md-toggle').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state.mdRendered = !state.mdRendered;
    $('btn-md-toggle').textContent = state.mdRendered ? '📝 Raw' : '👁 Rendered';
    if (state.selectedPath) {
        const path = state.selectedPath;
        const content = state.files[path];
        const lines = content.split('\n');
        const needsTrunc = lines.length > LINE_LIMIT;
        const displayContent = needsTrunc ? lines.slice(0, LINE_LIMIT).join('\n') : content;
        _renderContent(displayContent, detectLang(path), path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase(), true);
    }
});

// ── HTML toggle ───────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-html-toggle').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state.htmlRendered = !state.htmlRendered;
    $('btn-html-toggle').textContent = state.htmlRendered ? '📝 Raw' : '👁 Preview';
    if (state.selectedPath) {
        const path = state.selectedPath;
        const content = state.files[path];
        const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
        const lines = content.split('\n');
        const needsTrunc = lines.length > LINE_LIMIT;
        const displayContent = needsTrunc ? lines.slice(0, LINE_LIMIT).join('\n') : content;
        _renderContent(displayContent, detectLang(path), ext, false);
    }
});

// ── Copy ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-copy-file').addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (!state.selectedPath) return;
    const content = state.files[state.selectedPath];
    try {
        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(content);
        showToast();
    } catch {
        const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
        ta.value = content;
        document.body.appendChild(ta);
        ta.select();
        document.execCommand('copy');
        ta.remove();
        showToast();
    }
});

function showToast() {
    const t = $('copy-toast');
    t.classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 1800);
}

// ── Show all lines ────────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-show-all').addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (!state.selectedPath) return;
    $('truncation-notice').style.display = 'none';
    const path = state.selectedPath;
    const content = state.fullContent[path];
    const lang = detectLang(path);
    const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
    _renderContent(content, lang, ext, ext === 'md' && state.mdRendered);
});

// ── Load packed text ──────────────────────────────────────────
function loadPacked(text, sourceName) {
    if (!text || !text.trim()) {
        showLandingNotice('No content provided.', 'error');
        return;
    }

    const files = parsePacked(text);
    const count = Object.keys(files).length;

    if (count === 0) {
        showLandingNotice(
            'No valid file delimiters found. Expected lines like:<br><code>&lt;!-- ==== FILE: path/file.ext ==== --&gt;</code>',
            'error'
        );
        return;
    }

    state.files = files;
    state.selectedPath = null;
    state.fullContent = {};

    const firstPath = Object.keys(files)[0];
    state.rootName = firstPath.split('/')[0] || sourceName || 'archive';

    treeContainer.innerHTML = '';
    const tree = buildTree(files);
    renderTreeNode(tree, 0, treeContainer);

    $('st-file-count').textContent = count;
    $('st-viewing').textContent = '—';
    $('st-lang').textContent = '—';
    $('st-lines').textContent = '—';
    $('sidebar-title').textContent = state.rootName;

    landing.style.display = 'none';
    viewer.classList.add('active');
    $('btn-download-zip').style.display = 'inline-flex';
    $('btn-reset').style.display = 'inline-flex';

    contentToolbar.style.display = 'none';
    breadcrumb.innerHTML = '';
    $('truncation-notice').style.display = 'none';
    codeWrapper.innerHTML = '';
    codeWrapper.appendChild(createWelcome());
}

function createWelcome() {
    const d = document.createElement('div');
    d.id = 'welcome';
    d.innerHTML = `<span class="welcome-icon">📄</span><p>Select a file from the tree to view its contents</p>`;
    return d;
}

// ── ZIP download ───────────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-download-zip').addEventListener('click', async () => {
    const zip = new JSZip();
    for (const [path, content] of Object.entries(state.files)) {
        zip.file(path, content);
    }
    const blob = await zip.generateAsync({ type: 'blob' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = `${state.rootName}.zip`;
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
});

// ── Reset ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state.files = {};
    state.selectedPath = null;
    state.rootName = '';
    viewer.classList.remove('active');
    landing.style.display = '';
    $('btn-download-zip').style.display = 'none';
    $('btn-reset').style.display = 'none';
    $('landing-notice').style.display = 'none';
    $('st-file-count').textContent = '—';
    $('st-viewing').textContent = '—';
    $('st-lang').textContent = '—';
    $('st-lines').textContent = '—';
    $('url-input').value = '';
    $('landing-url').value = '';
    $('file-input').value = '';
    exitFullscreen();
    renderUrlHistory();
});

// ── File input ────────────────────────────────────────────────
$('file-input').addEventListener('change', e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = ev => loadPacked(ev.target.result, file.name.replace(/\.txt$/, ''));
    reader.readAsText(file);
    e.target.value = '';
});

function triggerFilePicker() { $('file-input').click(); }

$('btn-browse-landing').addEventListener('click', triggerFilePicker);
$('btn-browse-header').addEventListener('click', triggerFilePicker);

// Drag & drop
const dropZone = $('drop-zone');
dropZone.addEventListener('click', triggerFilePicker);
dropZone.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') triggerFilePicker(); });

['dragenter','dragover'].forEach(ev => {
    dropZone.addEventListener(ev, e => { e.preventDefault(); dropZone.classList.add('drag-over'); });
});
['dragleave','drop'].forEach(ev => {
    dropZone.addEventListener(ev, e => { e.preventDefault(); dropZone.classList.remove('drag-over'); });
});
dropZone.addEventListener('drop', e => {
    const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = ev => loadPacked(ev.target.result, file.name.replace(/\.txt$/, ''));
    reader.readAsText(file);
});

// ── Paste ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function pasteContent() {
    try {
        const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();
        if (!text.trim()) {
            showLandingNotice('Clipboard is empty or contains no text.', 'warn');
            return;
        }
        loadPacked(text, 'pasted');
    } catch {
        showLandingNotice('Could not read clipboard. Try using Ctrl+V in the URL field, or use drag & drop.', 'warn');
    }
}

$('btn-paste-landing').addEventListener('click', pasteContent);
$('btn-paste-header').addEventListener('click', pasteContent);

document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
    if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'v') {
        const active = document.activeElement;
        const isInput = active && (active.tagName === 'INPUT' || active.tagName === 'TEXTAREA');
        if (!isInput) {
            e.preventDefault();
            pasteContent();
        }
    }
});

// ── URL fetch ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function fetchUrl(rawUrl) {
    let url = rawUrl.trim();
    if (!url) return;

    if (!url.startsWith('http://') && !url.startsWith('https://')) {
        url = 'https://' + url;
    }

    landing.style.display = 'flex';
    const spinner = document.createElement('div');
    spinner.className = 'spinner-wrap';
    spinner.id = 'fetch-spinner';
    spinner.innerHTML = `<div class="spinner"></div><span>Fetching from URL…</span>`;
    landing.appendChild(spinner);

    try {
        const res = await fetch(url);
        if (!res.ok) {
            throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status} — ${res.statusText}`);
        }
        const text = await res.text();
        landing.removeChild(spinner);

        // ▼ Save to localStorage (unique links only)
        saveLink(url);

        loadPacked(text, url.split('/').pop().replace(/\.txt$/, '') || 'fetched');
    } catch (err) {
        landing.removeChild(spinner);
        let msg = `Failed to fetch: ${err.message}.`;
        if (err.message.toLowerCase().includes('cors') || err.message.toLowerCase().includes('failed to fetch')) {
            msg += ' <strong>CORS error</strong> — the server does not allow browser fetches. Try downloading the file and using drag &amp; drop instead.';
        }
        showLandingNotice(msg, 'error');
    }
}

$('btn-fetch-url').addEventListener('click', () => fetchUrl($('url-input').value));
$('url-input').addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') fetchUrl($('url-input').value); });

$('btn-fetch-landing').addEventListener('click', () => fetchUrl($('landing-url').value));
$('landing-url').addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') fetchUrl($('landing-url').value); });

// ── Notices ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
function showLandingNotice(html, type) {
    const n = $('landing-notice');
    n.className = `notice ${type}`;
    n.innerHTML = html;
    n.style.display = 'block';
}

// ── Expand / Collapse all ─────────────────────────────────────
$('btn-expand-all').addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-children').forEach(el => el.classList.add('open'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-arrow').forEach(el => el.classList.add('open'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-item .tree-icon').forEach(el => {
        if (el.textContent === '📁') el.textContent = '📂';
    });
});

$('btn-collapse-all').addEventListener('click', () => {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-children').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('open'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-arrow').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('open'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.tree-item .tree-icon').forEach(el => {
        if (el.textContent === '📂') el.textContent = '📁';
    });
});

// ── Hamburger (mobile) ────────────────────────────────────────
$('hamburger').addEventListener('click', () => {
    state.sidebarOpen = !state.sidebarOpen;
    sidebar.classList.toggle('open', state.sidebarOpen);
});

document.addEventListener('click', e => {
    if (window.innerWidth <= 680 && state.sidebarOpen) {
        if (!sidebar.contains(e.target) && e.target !== $('hamburger')) {
            sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            state.sidebarOpen = false;
        }
    }
});

// ── Resizer (drag to resize sidebar) ──────────────────────────
(function() {
    let dragging = false;
    let startX, startW;

    resizer.addEventListener('mousedown', e => {
        dragging = true;
        startX = e.clientX;
        startW = sidebar.getBoundingClientRect().width;
        resizer.classList.add('dragging');
        document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
        document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
    });

    document.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
        if (!dragging) return;
        const delta = e.clientX - startX;
        const newW = Math.max(160, Math.min(500, startW + delta));
        sidebar.style.width = newW + 'px';
        sidebar.style.minWidth = newW + 'px';
        sidebar.style.maxWidth = newW + 'px';
    });

    document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
        if (!dragging) return;
        dragging = false;
        resizer.classList.remove('dragging');
        document.body.style.cursor = '';
        document.body.style.userSelect = '';
        // Persist sidebar width
        const finalW = sidebar.getBoundingClientRect().width;
        if (finalW >= 160 && finalW <= 500) {
            localStorage.setItem('phase_sidebar_width', Math.round(finalW));
        }
    });
})();

// ── hljs config ───────────────────────────────────────────────
hljs.configure({ tabReplace: '    ' });

// ── Disable GFM strikethrough (~ used for "approximately") ────
marked.use({ tokenizer: { del() {} } });
</script>
</body>
</html>
